### [1] [Loss of positive definiteness is a symptom, not the cause, of high-Weissenberg-number breakdown](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15334)
*Yuan Yu,Lanjin Lian,Feiyang Chu*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 该论文挑战了“高Weissenberg数下构型张量失去对称正定性（SPD）必然导致数值崩溃”的传统观点。作者发现，在存在溶剂粘度（β>0）的情况下，即使构型张量变为不定态，问题仍然是局部适定的。他们推导了不定态增长率的定量理论，发现应力扩散可以截止增长率，而溶剂粘度消失时才会重现经典的σ∝k灾难。通过行列式恒等式证明，不定性在时间尺度λ/2内会自愈合，因此持续的不定性实际上是重现它的截断误差的度量。谱方法和格子Boltzmann测试验证了阈值和溶剂分数反转效应。在四辊试验中，强制保持SPD虽然将失稳延迟了15个对流时间，但使驻点Wi数降低了30%。在五种耦合方案中，一种局部二阶矩应力源方案在Wi=50时仍保持稳定，尽管detA≈-8.5×10⁵；而散度耦合变体在t*=47时失败。幸存方案在Wi=10和20时与公布基准值的误差分别为0.05%和0.18%。因此，失去正定性既不是数值崩溃的必要条件也不是充分条件：离散耦合方式才是决定性因素，不定性只是分辨率度量，作者为此提供了运行时监控工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高Weissenberg数（Wi）下的数值崩溃问题长期困扰着粘弹性流体动力学研究。传统观点认为崩溃源于构型张量失去对称正定性（SPD），但这一结论基于Maxwell型模型（无溶剂粘度）的简化分析。现实中大多数流体含有溶剂粘度（β>0），作者希望重新审视在更实际的溶剂存在条件下，构型张量不定态是否真的必然导致数值崩溃，并建立定量理论来预测和解释这一现象。

Method: 采用理论分析与数值实验相结合的方法。理论方面：(1) 对含溶剂粘度的模型进行冻结系数分析，推导增长率与波数的关系；(2) 推导不定态增长率的统一上界和方向分辨的不稳定性阈值λ_min(A) < -β/(1-β)；(3) 利用行列式恒等式证明不定性的自愈合性质。数值方面：(4) 采用光谱方法和格子Boltzmann方法进行验证；(5) 在四辊流动设置中进行干预实验，对比强制保持SPD与允许不定态的策略；(6) 测试五种不同的离散耦合方案，观察其在高Wi数下的稳定性表现。

Result: (1) 冻结系数分析给出增长率被波数一致有界，方向分辨的不稳定性阈值为λ_min(A) < -β/(1-β)；(2) 应力扩散提供闭合形式的截止，溶剂粘度消失时恢复经典的σ∝k灾难；(3) 行列式恒等式表明不定性在时间尺度λ/2内自愈合，持续不定性实为截断误差的度量；(4) 光谱和格子Boltzmann测试验证了阈值和溶剂分数反转效应；(5) 强制SPD将失稳延迟15个对流时间，但驻点Wi数降低30%；(6) 局部二阶矩应力源方案在Wi=50、detA≈-8.5×10⁵时仍稳定，散度耦合方案在t*=47失败；(7) 幸存方案复现基准值精度在0.05%（Wi=10）和0.18%（Wi=20）以内。

Conclusion: 失去对称正定性既不是高Weissenberg数下数值崩溃的必然原因，也不是其必要条件。崩溃的关键在于离散耦合方式的选择，而非构型张量的正定性状态。不定性本身只是离散误差的度量指标，可以用作运行时监控工具。这一发现颠覆了粘弹性流体数值模拟领域的传统认知，为设计更鲁棒的高Wi数数值方案提供了理论依据和实践指导。

Abstract: Numerical breakdown at high Weissenberg number is often attributed to loss of symmetric positive definiteness (SPD) of the conformation tensor. That conclusion follows from Maxwell-type models without solvent viscosity. With solvent fraction $β>0$, the initial-value problem is locally well posed for arbitrary symmetric stress. We derive the missing quantitative theory for indefinite states and test its computational consequences. Frozen-coefficient analysis gives a growth rate uniformly bounded in wavenumber and the direction-resolved instability threshold $λ_{\min}(A)<-β/(1-β)$; stress diffusion supplies a closed-form cutoff, while the classical $σ\propto k$ catastrophe is recovered as solvent viscosity vanishes. A determinant identity shows that violations self-heal on the timescale $λ/2$, so persistent violations measure the truncation error that recreates them. Spectral and lattice Boltzmann tests reproduce the threshold, solvent-fraction reversal, and resolution independence. In four-roll-mill interventions, enforcing SPD delays blow-up by 15 convective times but reduces the stagnation-point Weissenberg number by 30%. Across five coupling schemes, a local second-moment stress source remains stable through the full budget at $\mathrm{Wi}=50$ while carrying $\det A\approx-8.5\times10^5$; the divergence-coupled variant fails at $t^*=47$. The surviving scheme matches published benchmarks within 0.05% and 0.18% at $\mathrm{Wi}=10$ and 20. Thus loss of positive definiteness is neither necessary nor sufficient for breakdown: the discrete coupling route decides, and the violation is a resolution gauge for which we provide run-time monitors.

</details>


### [2] [Atomic Design Transformer: Scaffold-Conditioned 3D Molecule Generation via xTB-Reward Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15918)
*Takao Kotani*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种SE(3)不变性的原子自回归Transformer（ADT），用于三维分子生成。该方法通过局部坐标系编码原子位置实现SE(3)不变性，并引入xTB拓扑保持率（XTP）作为评估指标。预训练模型在GEOM-Drugs数据集上达到约54%的XTP和约50%的有效分子产率；通过强化学习（RLVR）优化后，XTP提升至约98%，有效分子产率提升至约95%。此外，还提出了逆运动学Transformer以解决大分子离散误差累积问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有三维分子生成方法通常在SE(3)等变性和生成质量之间存在权衡，且缺乏能够直接验证生成分子化学有效性和拓扑保持性的可靠评估指标。本文旨在设计一种兼具SE(3)不变性、高效自回归生成能力，并能通过可验证奖励优化生成质量的分子生成框架。

Method: 提出Atomic Design Transformer (ADT)，采用因果Transformer作为骨干网络，通过将新原子的位置编码在已放置原子的局部坐标系中实现SE(3)不变性。原子和键信息通过token流直接编码，无需独立分配键序。引入xTB拓扑保持率（XTP）作为评估指标，使用GFN2方法进行几何松弛后检查分子拓扑是否保持不变。训练分两阶段：先在GEOM-Drugs数据集上预训练，再通过强化学习（RLVR）以xTB计算结果作为奖励进行优化。同时提出逆运动学Transformer解决大分子生成中的离散误差问题。

Result: 预训练ADT在7种药物相关支架的条件生成任务中，XTP达到约54%，有效分子产率N^gen/N达到约50%。经过RLVR强化学习后，XTP提升至约98%，N^gen/N提升至约95%，且分子大小和组成分布与GEOM-Drugs数据集基本一致。

Conclusion: ADT通过局部坐标token化设计和强化学习优化，实现了高质量的三维分子直接生成，在拓扑保持性和化学有效性方面表现出色。逆运动学Transformer进一步扩展了该方法对大分子的适用性。该工作展示了结合物理验证奖励的强化学习在分子生成中的有效性。

Abstract: We present an SE(3)-invariant transformer for 3D-molecule generation,
  the Atomic Design Transformer (ADT). ADT places atoms one
  at a time, autoregressively. SE(3) invariance is achieved by
  tokenization: each new atom's position is encoded in the local
  coordinate frame of a previously placed atom. The backbone is a plain
  causal transformer. The token stream fully specifies a 3D structure
  together with its chemical-bond graph G, without any bond-order
  assignment. To score generated molecules we introduce the xTB
  topology-preservation rate (XTP): the fraction of molecules for
  which an xTB GFN2 relaxation preserves G specified by the token stream.
  For XTP-accepted molecules we also report the
  relaxation energy and the root mean square of the atomic displacement (RMSD). We evaluate
  two ADT models. The first is ADT pretrained on the GEOM-Drugs
  $\le\!30$-heavy-atom dataset; we benchmark scaffold-conditioned 3D
  generation across seven drug-like scaffolds from the model. It
  reaches an XTP of ${\sim}54\%$ and a valid-molecule yield
  $N^{\mathrm{gen}}/N$ of ${\sim}50\%$, where $N^{\mathrm{gen}}/N$ is the
  fraction of samples that are distinct, topology-preserving, and
  chemically valid. The second model continues from the first by
  reinforcement learning against the verifiable xTB reward (RLVR), using
  no external molecules. RLVR raises XTP to ${\sim}98\%$ and
  $N^{\mathrm{gen}}/N$ to ${\sim}95\%$, while approximately preserving the
  GEOM-Drugs size and composition distributions. Finally, we present
  an Inverse-Kinematics Transformer that recovers XTP for large molecules, where discretization error accumulates. ADT thus enables direct 3D generation.

</details>


### [3] [CADAQUES: A Cost-Aware Dual Architecture for Query-Efficient Autonomous Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16127)
*Jorge Bravo-Abad*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: CADAQUES 是一个将成本作为一等原语的开源 Python 自主发现框架，通过分离 Oracle（回答查询）和 Driver（提出查询）两个协议，并使用向量值预算追踪墙时间、CPU 小时、货币成本和语言模型代币，实现了对发现循环中查询成本和决策成本的显式计量与管理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自主发现系统多沿用数值优化的控制结构：固定迭代次数、编程接口中忽略查询成本、视决策为免费。然而实际中查询成本可能相差数个数量级，且基于大语言模型或昂贵代理模型的规划器本身也消耗大量资源，亟需一种将成本显式纳入一等的框架。

Method: 将发现循环解耦为两个结构协议：Oracle（回答查询）和 Driver（提出查询）。引入向量值预算（墙时间、CPU 小时、货币成本、LM 代币），对评估和决策均计费。采用仅追加的分类账记录每笔交易执行前申报的成本和执行后结算的成本，使两者差异成为可观测属性。

Result: 在二维伊辛模型临界温度定位任务上，使用低成本低保真度查询探索、高成本高保真度查询精炼的策略比全程高保真度策略错误更低且方差更小；计量开销仅数十微秒每次迭代，比最便宜的 oracle 查询低三个数量级。

Conclusion: CADAQUES 证明了将成本作为一等原语设计自主发现循环在架构上是可行的，且在实际噪声场景下能引导更优的资源分配策略，框架本身的开销可忽略不计。

Abstract: Autonomous discovery systems couple a resource that answers queries (a simulator, instrument, or analytic model) to an algorithm that selects what to query next. Most software frameworks for this loop inherit the control structure of numerical optimization: campaigns run for a fixed number of iterations, query costs are absent from the programming interface, and decision-making is treated as free. In practice, queries may differ in cost by orders of magnitude, and planners built on large language models or expensive surrogates consume resources of their own. Here we present CADAQUES, an open-source Python framework built on one architectural principle: cost is a first-class primitive of the discovery loop. CADAQUES separates the loop into two structural protocols, an Oracle that answers queries and a Driver that proposes them, and charges both evaluations and decisions against a common vector-valued budget spanning wall time, CPU hours, monetary cost, and language model tokens. An append-only ledger records, for each transaction, the cost declared before execution and the cost settled afterwards, making their discrepancy an observable property of the campaign. We evaluate the architecture by locating the critical temperature of the two-dimensional Ising model from noisy finite-size estimates against the exact thermodynamic-limit reference. In this noisy setting, strategies that concentrate around the best observed result can be misled by noise-induced peaks, whereas a schedule that explores with cheap low-fidelity queries and refines with higher-fidelity ones yields lower and less variable errors than high fidelity throughout, at the studied budget scale. Metering adds tens of microseconds per iteration, three orders of magnitude below the cheapest oracle query. The framework is MIT-licensed and archived at Zenodo (doi:10.5281/zenodo.21293589).

</details>

### [4] [A persistent-homology-Gaussian prior for solving infinite-dimensional Bayesian inverse scattering problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15289)
*Zhiyuan Wang,Hang Qi,Xiaofei Guan,Zhiliang Deng,Xiaomei Yang*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文针对声学障碍散射反问题，提出了一种持久同调-高斯（PHG）先验，该先验通过Gibbs倾斜将基于持久性的加权正则化项与周期高斯参考测度结合，在无穷维贝叶斯框架下实现了对间断或剧烈变化目标函数的重建，并证明了后验测度的适定性及有限维近似的收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统高斯先验无法有效重构具有间断或剧烈变化的目标函数（如障碍物重建），而混合先验虽具潜力但在工程应用中缺乏理论严谨且计算可行的框架。

Method: 提出PHG先验：将持久同调加权的正则化项通过Gibbs倾斜与周期高斯参考测度结合；采用单位圆上的对数径向函数表示复杂边界；利用pCN方法进行后验采样。

Result: 在Hellinger、总变差和Wasserstein-p度量下证明了后验测度的适定性；获得了有限维后验近似的收敛性；数值实验表明PHG先验在更广泛的噪声条件下实现了准确稳定的重建，显式控制了多尺度拓扑特征，性能优于传统先验。

Conclusion: PHG先验为无穷维贝叶斯反问题中处理间断或剧烈变化目标提供了一种理论完善且计算可行的框架，在声学障碍散射反问题中展现出优越的重建性能。

Abstract: Bayesian inference methods have been developed to address inverse problems in function spaces where the unknown parameters are of infinite dimension. However, conventional Gaussian priors remain inadequate for reconstructing discontinuous or sharply varying target functions encountered in practical applications like obstacle reconstruction. Although hybrid priors have emerged as a promising solution, significant challenges remain in developing theoretically rigorous and computationally tractable frameworks in engineering applications. To address these issues, we propose a persistent-homology-Gaussian (PHG) prior for solving the acoustic obstacle scattering inverse problem in the infinite-dimensional Bayesian setting, which combines a weighted persistence-based regularization term with a periodic Gaussian reference measure through a Gibbs tilt. Then, the complex boundary is represented by a log-radial function on the unit circle, so that the reconstruction from far-field data is formulated as a function-space inverse problem. The well-posedness of the resulting posterior measure is established in the Hellinger, total variation, and Wasserstein-\(p\) metrics. Furthermore, the convergence of finite-dimensional posterior approximations is obtained, and posterior sampling is performed by a preconditioned Crank--Nicolson (pCN) method. Numerical experiments show that the proposed PHG prior yields accurate and stable reconstructions under more extensive noisy conditions, providing explicit control of multiscale topological features and better performance compared to other conventional priors.

</details>


### [5] [An FFT-Based Direct Splitting Method for Efficient Micromagnetic Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15290)
*Hang Qi,Changqing Ye,Xiaofei Guan*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文针对Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert方程数值模拟的高计算成本问题，通过重新审视切平面公式，将离散问题转化为广义鞍点系统，并开发了基于FFT和分裂迭代法的无矩阵预处理子，实现了高效、可扩展的微磁模拟框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert方程因非线性、非凸单位长度约束及非局部场贡献，数值模拟极具挑战。现有隐式/半隐式格式虽无条件稳定，但需反复求解非线性或线性化系统，计算成本高昂。

Method: 重新审视切平面公式，将每时间步离散问题化为广义鞍点系统；结合FFT技术与分裂迭代法，开发无矩阵预处理子；利用快速泊松求解器直接高效实现分裂分量；进一步引入Crank-Nicolson格式以增强几何一致性并减少投影步。

Result: 大量2D和3D数值实验验证了该框架的约束保持准确性、计算效率提升和求解器鲁棒性；方法在大规模微磁模拟中展现出良好的可扩展性。

Conclusion: 提出的预处理框架能有效处理LLG方程数值求解的计算瓶颈，适用于复杂磁系统的实际应用。

Abstract: The Landau--Lifshitz--Gilbert equation poses significant challenges for numerical simulation due to its nonlinearity, nonconvex unit-length constraint, and nonlocal field contributions. Existing implicit or semi-implicit schemes exhibit unconditional stability but require repeated solution of nonlinear or linearized systems, resulting in high computational costs. In this work, we revisit the tangent plane formulation and show that the resulting discrete problem at each time step can be written as a generalized saddle-point system. Exploiting this structure, we develop a matrix-free preconditioner for the implicit Euler scheme by combining FFT-based techniques with a splitting iteration method. We show that each component in the splitting method can be efficiently implemented in a direct fashion via fast Poisson solvers, enabling the design of an efficient preconditioner for iterative solvers. To enhance geometric consistency of the tangent vector and reduce projection steps, a Crank--Nicolson scheme is further investigated, retaining the same algorithmic structure as the Euler scheme, thus allowing direct reuse of preconditioners and solvers. Extensive 2D and 3D numerical experiments are conducted to validate the framework, demonstrating accurate constraint preservation, improved computational efficiency, and robust solver performance. The proposed approach is shown to scale effectively for large-scale micromagnetic simulations, making it suitable for practical applications in complex magnetic systems.

</details>


### [6] [A Physics-Informed Neural Network with a Modified Lorentzian Activation for Nonlocal Gradient-Flow Equations in Dynamic Density Functional Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15291)
*Dimitrios Gourzoulidis,Soumaya Elkantassi,Serafim Kalliadasis*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于物理信息的神经网络（PINN）框架，用于求解动态密度泛函理论（DDFT）中的非局部偏微分方程，通过改进的洛伦兹激活函数和预计算离散算子，在多个一维和二维算例中实现了比标准tanh更快的收敛和良好的物理一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DDFT中的非局部偏微分方程包含非线性项、非局部相互作用项和梯度流结构，标准PINN方法在处理这类方程时面临收敛缓慢和优化困难的问题，亟需针对性的改进方法。

Method: 提出了两个关键改进：(1) 修正洛伦兹激活函数——在小输入时近似线性，在大输入时衰减至零；(2) 预计算离散算子——高效计算训练中的非局部卷积项。在一维和二维共四个算例上进行测试，通过L1、L2、L∞误差以及质量守恒和自由能耗散评估精度与物理一致性。

Result: 所提激活函数相比标准tanh加速了收敛；整体框架与参考解（连续/间断Galerkin有限元解）吻合良好，并成功捕捉了预期的梯度流行为。

Conclusion: 该PINN框架在求解DDFT中的非局部梯度流方程方面展现了潜力，为处理同类复杂方程提供了有效工具。

Abstract: We develop a physics-informed neural network (PINN) framework for nonlocal partial differential equations arising in dynamic density functional theory (DDFT). Such equations are challenging for standard PINN methods because they involve nonlinearities, nonlocal interaction terms, and an underlying gradient-flow structure, often leading to slow convergence and difficult optimization. We adapt the PINN methodology to DDFT gradient-flow equations and introduce two computational components: a modified Lorentzian activation function that behaves approximately linearly for small inputs and decays toward zero as the input magnitude increases, and a precomputed discrete operator for evaluating the nonlocal convolution term efficiently during training. The method is tested on four examples in one and two space dimensions. In the first example, the exact stationary solution is known, while in the remaining cases the neural-network approximations are validated against reference solutions computed using continuous and discontinuous Galerkin finite element discretizations. Accuracy and physical consistency are assessed through $L^1$, $L^2$, and $L^\infty$ errors, together with mass conservation and free-energy dissipation. The results show that the proposed activation function accelerates convergence relative to the standard $\tanh$ function, while the overall framework maintains good agreement with the reference solutions and captures the expected gradient-flow behaviour. These findings demonstrate the potential of the proposed PINN framework for solving nonlocal gradient-flow equations arising in DDFT.

</details>


### [7] [A 3D-ACA accelerated time domain boundary element method for elastodynamics using FMM and $\mathcal{H}$-matrix techniques](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15292)
*Vibudha Lakshmi Keshava,Martin Schanz*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文针对线性弹性动力学的时域边界元法，采用广义卷积求积进行时间离散化，并提出3D-自适应交叉近似（3D-ACA）对拉普拉斯域中的BEM矩阵张量进行低秩压缩，结合H矩阵或快速多极方法进行空间压缩，通过算例验证了方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 降低时域边界元法在广义卷积求积框架下因需要处理多个复频率点而产生的高存储和计算成本。

Method: 采用广义卷积求积(gCQ)进行时间离散化；提出3D-自适应交叉近似(3D-ACA)对频率-空间三维张量进行低秩近似；在每层频率切片内，分别采用经典ACA的H矩阵方法或Chebyshev插值的快速多极方法(FMM)进行进一步压缩。

Result: 通过两个学术算例和感应电机结构振动分析，对所提方法进行了比较研究。

Conclusion: 3D-ACA结合H矩阵或FMM的空间压缩策略能有效降低时域边界元法的存储与计算开销，适用于弹性动力学问题。

Abstract: The time-domain Boundary Element Method (BEM) for linear elastodynamics with vanishing initial conditions is considered. Spatial discretization uses standard low-order boundary elements, while temporal discretization employs the generalized Convolution Quadrature (gCQ) method. The gCQ framework requires evaluating BEM matrices in the Laplace domain at several complex frequencies along a chosen contour, producing a three-dimensional tensor with one spatial matrix slice per frequency. To reduce storage and computational cost, a low rank approximation of the tensor is computed using 3D-Adaptive Cross Approximation (3D-ACA), extending the classical ACA to handle both the additional frequency dimension and the tensorial structure of elastodynamics. Within each frequency slice, the BEM matrices are further compressed using either the classical ACA algorithm using the $\mathcal{H}$-matrix approach or a Chebyshev interpolation based Fast Multipole Method (FMM). A comparative study of all proposed methods is carried out using two academic examples, and the structural vibration of an induction machine is analyzed.

</details>


### [8] [RCLUPPr: a new randomized CholeskyQR with LU preconditioning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15561)
*Haoran Guan,Zhenyu Zou,Yufeng Wei,Yipei Chen,Peiting You,Yuwei Fan*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文对RCLUPPr算法进行了完整的舍入误差分析。RCLUPPr是一种新型随机化CholeskyQR类算法，通过对高瘦矩阵X直接执行带部分选主元的LU分解（LUPP），并将其作为预处理步骤（而非后处理步骤），显著减少了误差传播。严格证明了该算法对病态矩阵的适用性优于现有CholeskyQR类算法，且在混合精度计算中保持稳定精确，并提出了实际加速策略。大量数值实验验证了理论结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RCLUPP算法先进行矩阵草图再执行LUPP分解，误差传播较大；而其他CholeskyQR类算法对病态矩阵的适用性有限。本文旨在设计一种更稳定的算法，使其在病态矩阵和混合精度环境下仍能保持高精度和稳定性。

Method: 将LUPP分解作为预处理步骤（RCLUPPr），先进行LUPP再执行后续随机化CholeskyQR流程，以减小误差传播；在此基础上进行完整的舍入误差分析，证明其数值稳定性；并提出实际加速策略（如优化矩阵乘法实现、自适应精度选择等）。

Result: 理论分析证明RCLUPPr对病态矩阵的适用性显著优于现有CholeskyQR类算法，在混合精度运算中保持稳定精确；实际加速策略有效提升了效率；单精度、双精度及混合精度环境下的数值实验验证了算法的鲁棒性和实用性。

Conclusion: RCLUPPr通过将LUPP前置作为预处理步骤，在病态矩阵处理和混合精度计算方面取得了明显优势，是一种稳健且实用的CholeskyQR类算法，适用于高瘦矩阵的数值计算场景。

Abstract: In this work, we present the comprehensive rounding error analysis of RCLUPPr proposed in \cite{RCLUPP}, which is a novel randomized CholeskyQR-type algorithm performing LU decomposition with partial pivoting (LUPP decomposition) directly on the tall-skinny $X\in\mathbb{R}^{m\times n}$ with $m \ge n$ and $\mbox{rank}(X)=n$. In contrast to the existing RCLUPP in \cite{RCLUPP}, which applies matrix sketching before LUPP decomposition, RCLUPPr places LUPP decomposition as a preconditioning step first, significantly reducing error propagation. Our analysis rigorously proves that RCLUPPr enjoys markedly better applicability to the ill-conditioned matrices than the existing CholeskyQR-type algorithms and remains stable and accurate in the mixed-precision arithmetic. We further propose practical acceleration strategies in the real implementations of RCLUPPr. Extensive numerical experiments on the real-world problems confirm the theoretical results in this work, demonstrating the robustness and practicality of RCLUPPr in the single, double, and the mixed-precision architecture.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有判断线性自伴微分代数系统渐近稳定性的方法（基于线性化、矩阵方程或广义Bézoutians）复杂度高（O(d² n³)或O(d³ n³)），需要更高效的算法。

Method: 基于Hermitian矩阵多项式P(λ)的数值域，建立若干新的充分条件，设计复杂度为O(d n³)的算法，核心依赖于Cholesky分解和最大特征值计算等高效数值线性代数运算。

Result: 新算法复杂度为O(d n³)，显著低于现有方法；通过数值实验验证了计算优势，即使在中等d或n下也能体现。

Conclusion: 基于数值域的充分条件为自伴微分代数系统的稳定性判断提供了新的高效途径，所提算法在理论上和实验上均展现出优越的计算性能。

Abstract: Assessing the asymptotic stability of linear self-adjoint homogeneous systems of differential-algebraic equations requires testing the Hurwitz stability of the associated Hermitian matrix polynomial $P(λ)$. Tests for known necessary and sufficient conditions rely on linearizations and eigensolvers, solving matrix equations and testing matrix inequalities, or generalized Bézoutians, and scale with either $O(d^2 n^3)$ or $O(d^3n^3)$ complexity, where $d$ and $n$ are the degree and size of $P(λ)$, respectively. We establish several novel sufficient conditions for stability, based on the numerical range of $P(λ)$. Based on the new results, we propose algorithms with $O(d n^3)$ asymptotic complexity. Our methods rely on very efficient core numerical linear algebra routines, such as the Cholesky decomposition of $n \times n$ matrices or the computation of the largest eigenvalue of $n \times n$ definite pencils. Therefore, a significant computational advantage can be expected in favor of the proposed approach even for moderate values of $d$ or $n$, and we verify this with numerical experiments.

The hyperbolic terms are approximated by a local Lax--Friedrichs flux, while viscosity acts on the momentum variables through a penalty law $μ_e=σh_e^{-β}$. The standard choice $β=1$ and the super-penalized choice $β=3$ are compared with a symmetric interior-penalty Galerkin reference. For the diffusion form, we establish consistency, continuity for $β\ge 1$, and an exact coercivity identity in the momentum DG seminorm. Manufactured-solution tests show that super-penalization can recover the expected momentum $L^2$ accuracy, whereas the coupled geopotential variable need not exhibit the same improvement. Rotating and topography-aware tests further show that the standard scaling generally gives the better accuracy-cost compromise for the explicit implementation considered here.

### [11] [A Statistical Formulation Gap for Nonlinear Multiscale Physics-Informed Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15702)
*Ronald Katende*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文证明了非线性多尺度椭圆方程的物理信息学习中存在有限样本公式间隙。针对系数在ε尺度振荡的一致单调散度形式方程，推导了边界兼容的变分神经求解器的有限宽度、有限样本和有限迭代误差界。一维周期扩散方程中，强残差的经验Rademacher复杂度下界为(ε√N)^{-1}的常数倍，而变分能量复杂度上界为N^{-1/2}的常数倍且与ε无关。数值实验验证了理论指数。结果表明，对微观系数求导会产生有限样本统计病态，变分公式消除了统计惩罚但未消除多尺度逼近问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究物理信息神经网络（PINNs）在多尺度问题中的有限样本理论性质，特别是揭示不同公式（强形式残差与变分能量）在统计复杂度上的本质差异，以及多尺度逼近带来的根本性困难。

Method: 理论分析：推导有限样本误差界，证明Rademacher复杂度下界和上界；数值实验：对一维周期扩散方程进行数值拟合验证理论指数。

Result: 强残差经验Rademacher复杂度下界为(ε√N)^{-1}的常数倍，平方强残差损失下界为(ε²√N)^{-1}的常数倍，变分能量复杂度上界为N^{-1/2}的常数倍且与ε无关。数值拟合指数为0.9971、1.9860和-0.0028。

Conclusion: 对微观系数进行微分操作会导致有限样本统计病态（小ε时复杂度爆炸）；变分公式虽能消除此统计惩罚，但无法消除多尺度逼近这一独立问题，两者共同构成物理信息学习的根本性挑战。

Abstract: We prove a finite-sample formulation gap for physics-informed learning of nonlinear multiscale elliptic equations. For a uniformly monotone divergence-form class with coefficients oscillating at scale $ε$, we derive a finite-width, finite-sample, and finite-iteration error bound for a boundary-compatible variational neural solver. Its stability, sampling, and optimization constants are independent of $ε$, while all unresolved scale dependence is isolated in the best-approximation error.
  We then construct a minimal obstruction witness for a one-dimensional periodic diffusion equation with cubic reaction. Already on the one-parameter family $v_c(x)=cx(1-x)$, the empirical Rademacher complexity of the strong residual is bounded below by a constant multiple of $(ε\sqrt{N})^{-1}$, while that of the squared strong-residual loss is bounded below by a constant multiple of $(ε^2\sqrt{N})^{-1}$. These are optimizer-independent properties of the sampled residual and loss classes, rather than neural-tangent-kernel conditioning statements. The corresponding variational energy complexity is bounded above by a constant multiple of $N^{-1/2}$ uniformly in $ε$.
  A tensor-product construction shows that the same obstruction rates persist in every spatial dimension. Numerical evaluation gives fitted exponents $0.9971$, $1.9860$, and $-0.0028$ for the strong residual, squared strong loss, and variational energy, respectively. Thus, differentiating the microscopic coefficient creates finite-sample statistical ill-conditioning. The variational formulation removes this statistical penalty but does not remove the separate multiscale approximation problem.

### [12] [A zero-one law for one-shot system identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15832)
*Nicolas Boullé,Diana Halikias,Samuel E. Otto,Alex Townsend*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文研究线性参数化解析系统的单次实验可辨识性，证明了一个尖锐的零一律：要么没有输入能唯一确定系数，要么几乎所有的随机非退化高斯输入都能唯一确定。该结论将单次系统辨识简化为一个关于退化输入的问题，并为恢复的模型提供后验认证。数值实验展示了从单轨迹数据恢复动力系统、非线性PDE和结构化矩阵族，同时检测何时需要额外探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 回答一个基础性问题：能否通过单次实验（一个输入-响应对）唯一地辨识一个线性参数化的解析系统，并给出严格的理论条件。

Method: 利用线性参数化框架（字典项组合，如偏微分算子、动力系统），将可辨识性条件转化为字典项的线性无关性。通过分析非退化高斯测度下的随机输入，证明零一律：要么无解，要么几乎必然唯一解。

Result: 证明了尖锐的零一律；给出了单次实验可辨识的充要条件（字典项线性无关）；提供了后验认证机制；数值实验验证了方法在动力系统、非线性PDE和结构化矩阵族上的有效性。

Conclusion: 单次实验足以辨识一大类线性参数化系统，零一律极大地简化了可辨识性判断；当不可辨识时，可通过额外探测解决。

Abstract: Can a model be identified from one experiment? We study analytic systems that are linearly parameterized by a combination of prescribed dictionary terms, such as partial differential operators and dynamical systems. For a single input-response pair, recovery is possible exactly when the evaluated dictionary terms are linearly independent. We prove a sharp zero-one law: either no input uniquely determines the coefficients, or almost every random input sampled from a nondegenerate Gaussian measure does. This dichotomy reduces one-shot system identification to a question about degenerate inputs and provides an a posteriori certificate for any recovered model. Numerical examples recover dynamical systems, nonlinear partial differential equations, and structured matrix families from single trajectory data, while also detecting when an extra probe is necessary.

Abstract: This paper presents a practical guide to building lightweight neural-network surrogates for the plastic return-mapping process in concurrent multiscale (FE2) simulations. Rather than proposing a new architecture, we show how a deliberately simple feed-forward network, structured to mirror the classical return-mapping update, can replace the prohibitively expensive nested fine-scale solves that dominate the cost of conventional FE2 schemes based on FFT homogenization at the meso-scale. We walk through the full workflow: generating training data from incremental homogenization analyses, constructing a compact yet sufficient dataset, embedding material symmetries directly into the mapping, and deploying the trained network as a user-defined material subroutine (UMAT) in a standard finite-element solver -- enabling widespread use. A sensitivity study examines the model's robustness to data density, increment size, and mesh refinement, and we characterize the regimes in which the surrogate holds and where it breaks down. For the macroscopically isotropic, two-dimensional plane-stress setting considered here, the surrogate reproduces the reference response while reducing the per-analysis cost from hours to seconds with speed-ups up to 30,000 over standard FE2. The approach extends naturally to three dimensions and to weaker symmetry assumptions, given an appropriate sampling strategy and dataset.

Abstract: We propose a projected drift-randomized Milstein (PRM) method for stochastic differ ential equations with non-differentiable and super-linearly growing drift coefficients. Moreover, unlike existing first-order Milstein-type methods for SDEs with super-linearly growing drift coefficients, the proposed method does not require spatial differentiability of the drift coefficient. Under suitable polynomial Lipschitz and one-sided Lipschitz conditions on the drift, together with standard regularity assumptions on the diffusion, we establish a one-step mean-square stability estimate and derive the required local residual bounds. Abstract: The adaptive Bregman-Kaczmarz method recovers the exact, noise-free solution of a linear inverse problem even when every measurement it queries is corrupted, provided the corruption is fresh, independent and zero-mean. A block version was proposed for parallel hardware, but whether larger blocks actually converge faster was left open. We show the answer hinges on how the block is used: replacing the block sum with a block average collapses the analysis onto a single positive-semidefinite matrix, through which we prove that the guaranteed convergence improves monotonically with the batch size, with a total gain governed by the stable rank of the system matrix. We then address heterogeneous noise by introducing a noise-aware weighting that down-weights unreliable measurements, and prove it is strictly better than uniform weighting whenever the noise is not proportional to the row norms - a condition that essentially never holds in practice. The two improvements are compatible and their benefits combine. Finally, we show the adaptive step size interpolates automatically between a fast initial phase and a slowly vanishing tail that carries the error exactly to zero, and we explain how its hyperparameters can be estimated without knowing the true solution. Numerical experiments under sparse, heterogeneous noise illustrate these findings and confirm that the heuristic estimates produce effective step sizes.

</details>


### [16] [IMEX Schemes for Compressible Flow using Hybridizable Discontinuous Galerkin Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16044)
*Jan Ellmenreich,Edmond K. Shehadi,Philip L. Lederer*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于几何分裂的隐式-显式（IMEX）框架用于可压缩流动方程：在刚性区域使用混合化间断伽辽金（HDG）隐式方法，在非刚性区域使用间断伽辽金（DG）显式方法，通过适当的界面条件实现守恒耦合，并采用加性龙格-库塔（ARK）方案保持时间同步。数值实验表明该方法在空间和时间上均达到高阶精度，相比全显式DG方案可获得最高约50倍的加速比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可压缩流动方程中，几何诱导的刚性（如高纵横比网格或局部小尺度特征）使得全显式DG方法受限于严格的CFL条件，计算效率低下。现有IMEX方法多基于物理刚性（如低速流或反应流），而针对几何刚性的处理尚不充分。作者希望开发一种能够自动识别并分别处理几何刚性区域与非刚性区域的框架，以突破显式方法的稳定性限制，同时避免全局隐式方法的高计算成本。

Method: 1) **空间离散**：采用几何分裂策略，将计算域划分为隐式HDG区域（处理刚性网格）和显式DG区域（处理非刚性网格），界面处通过守恒型耦合条件实现通量匹配；2) **隐式格式**：研究了两种HDG变体——混合HDG（HDG-MX）和原始内罚HDG（HDG-IP）；3) **时间推进**：使用加性龙格-库塔（ARK）方案实现隐式和显式部分的同步，确保时间高阶精度；4) **性能分析**：通过一系列数值实验验证精度，并针对不同隐式区域选择进行加速比对比研究。

Result: 1) 所提出的IMEX方案在空间和时间上均实现了高阶精度（与设计精度一致）；2) 有效缓解了几何诱导的刚性限制；3) 在合理选择隐式区域的前提下，相比全显式DG方案可获得最高约50倍的加速比。

Conclusion: 几何分裂的IMEX-HDG/DG框架能够高效处理可压缩流动中的几何刚性，在保持高阶精度的同时大幅提升计算效率。HDG-MX和HDG-IP两种隐式格式均可行，且加速效果显著依赖于隐式区域的合理选择。

Abstract: In this work, we develop a geometry-split implicit-explicit (IMEX) framework for the compressible flow equations, wherein stiff regions are treated via an implicit hybridizable discontinuous Galerkin (HDG) method, while non-stiff regions are treated via an explicit discontinuous Galerkin (DG) method. Two implicit formulations are investigated: a mixed HDG method (HDG-MX) and a primal interior-penalty HDG method (HDG-IP). The spatial coupling between the implicit and explicit solutions is achieved in a conservative manner by appropriate interface conditions, while the temporal synchronization is maintained through the use of additive Runge-Kutta (ARK) schemes. We provide a detailed discussion on the computational performance of the resulting IMEX schemes. Verification and validation over a range of numerical experiments confirm that the proposed IMEX schemes achieve high-order accuracy in both space and time. Performance studies further indicate that the approach effectively alleviates geometry-induced stiffness and can provide speedups of up to approximately 50 relative to a fully explicit DG scheme, provided that the implicit region is chosen appropriately.

</details>


### [17] [The $hp$-FEM does not suffer from the pollution effect for piecewise-smooth Helmholtz problems with Gevrey regularity at boundaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16073)
*Jeffrey Galkowski,Mostafa Meliani,Euan A. Spence*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文证明了对于Helmholtz散射问题的hp-FEM方法，在解算子关于波数k多项式有界、系数分片光滑、边界为Gevrey类等条件下，当p≥1+ε log k且hk/p足够小时，方法拟最优且无污染效应。该结果将现有结论从解析系数/边界推广到更广泛的散射体类别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将现有hp-FEM分析（仅适用于解析系数和解析边界）推广到更一般的散射体类别，即系数分片光滑且边界为Gevrey类的情形，从而扩大方法的适用范围。

Method: 在完美匹配层截断的Helmholtz散射问题框架下，假设解算子关于k多项式有界，系数分片光滑，边界曲面为Gevrey类且边界上的系数及其法向导数同为Gevrey类，通过分析hp-FEM的收敛性，证明当p≥1+ε log k且hk/p足够小时，方法拟最优。

Result: 在上述广义条件下，hp-FEM达到拟最优，即不存在污染效应，只需p随log k线性增长且网格步长满足适当条件。

Conclusion: 该结果统一并推广了[Bernkopf等人2025]和[Galkowski等人2024]的结论，证明hp-FEM对更大类别的散射体（包括Dirichlet、Neumann、可穿透障碍及变系数情形）均能避免污染效应。

Abstract: We consider the $hp$-FEM applied to the Helmholtz scattering problem with wavenumber $k$, truncated with a perfectly-matched layer. The scatterer consists of a combination of Dirichlet, Neumann, and penetrable obstacles together with variable coefficients. Provided that the Helmholtz solution operator is polynomially bounded in $k$, all coefficients are piecewise smooth, all boundary surfaces are Gevrey and all coefficients restricted to boundary surfaces are Gevrey together with all their normal derivatives, we show that the $hp$-FEM is quasioptimal when $p\geq 1+\varepsilon \log k$ and $hk/p$ is sufficiently small; i.e., the $hp$-FEM does not suffer from the pollution effect. This result generalises the analogous results in both [Bernkopf, Chaumont-Frelet, Melenk 2025] (proved for piecewise analytic coefficients and analytic boundaries) and [Galkowski, Lafontaine, Spence, Wunsch 2024] (proved for smooth coefficients that are analytic near analytic obstacles) to a much larger class of scatterers.

</details>

### [18] [Structure of the Circular-Dyadic Convolution Error](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15293)
*Ben Fauber,Alireza Moradzadeh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了用Hadamard变换替代FFT计算循环卷积时产生的代数误差，发现该误差具有结构性：两个输入/输出位置完全无误差，误差算子近满秩但零空间仅对数维度，且期望误差可由单个对齐标量表达。除零误差子空间外，误差会使输出能量渐进翻倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hadamard变换因其实数值符号翻转（无需复数运算）在计算上优于FFT，但直接替代DFT计算循环卷积会引入代数误差。本文旨在系统地表征这一误差的结构和性质。

Method: 通过理论分析识别误差的精确抵消位置；计算误差算子的秩与零空间维度；通过随机滤波器平均得到期望误差的闭式表达式。

Result: 1) 两个输入和两个输出位置完全无误差；2) 误差算子近满秩，零空间仅对数维度；3) 期望误差由单个对齐标量决定；4) 除零误差子空间外，误差使输出能量渐进翻倍。

Conclusion: Hadamard替代FFT的误差是结构化的、可预测的，且由对齐程度决定，这为在特定场景下安全使用Hadamard变换提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Dyadic and circular convolution can both be computed in $O(N\log N)$ time using the Hadamard transform and the FFT-computed discrete Fourier transform (DFT), respectively. The Hadamard transform is preferable for its real-valued sign flips, yet its substitution for the DFT introduces algebraic error. We present three complementary results that characterize this error. First, we identify exact error cancellation: two input and two output positions are universally error-free, and no reordering of the output can eliminate this error. Second, the error operator is nearly full rank, while its null space has only logarithmic dimension. Third, the expected error is governed by a single alignment scalar, with a closed-form expression obtained by averaging over random filters. In general, the substitution error asymptotically doubles the output energy, except for filters in the universal zero-error subspace, which incur no error. Collectively, these results show that the substitution error is structured, predictable, and governed by alignment.

</details>


### [19] [Position: Quantum Program Generation Must Prioritize Validity Over Probabilistic Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15313)
*Junhao Song,Yu Zhou,William Knottenbelt,Yudong Cao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战"规模假设"在量子电路合成领域的适用性，指出单纯增加模型参数无法桥接量子电路的语法-语义鸿沟，后验过滤在数学上不可行。

Result: 分析表明，规模本身无法弥合量子电路的有效性差距，验证感知架构在模块化量子程序生成中更具可行性。

Conclusion: 量子电路生成应编码量子信息领域的任务特定规则，而非仅依赖模仿学习，验证感知架构是可行的前进方向。

Abstract: The scaling hypothesis assumes that increasing model parameters yields emergent reasoning capabilities. This position paper argues that applying this probabilistic paradigm to generic quantum circuit synthesis is a directional error. Unlike natural languages, quantum circuits require strict adherence to mathematical constraints that manifest a significant syntax-semantics gap. Training on unverified quantum programs means that models learn syntax but fail to capture the physical semantics of the Hilbert space. Since the valid subset of circuit designs decays exponentially with the number of qubits, post-hoc filtering is mathematically intractable. We propose a pivot from human-centric copilots to verifier-centric agents. We integrate hierarchical constraints, topological masks, and symbolic proxies directly into generation. Our analysis suggests that scale alone cannot bridge the validity gap. Verification-aware architectures offer a viable path for modular quantum program generation. These considerations point toward generation methods that encode task-specific rules of quantum information, rather than relying on imitation alone.

### [20] [A Transportable Threshold-Based Framework for Interpretable Classification of Medical Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15394)

TL;DR: 本文提出基于伯努利朴素贝叶斯（BNB）的统计可解释框架，通过χ²引导的统计二值化将连续医学数据转化为可解释的规则分类模型，在三个基准数据集上取得与复杂模型相当的AUC性能（0.800-0.984），并提供完整的概率校准与手工可复现的透明推理示例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑箱模型因缺乏可解释性和可重复性，限制了人工智能在医学领域的实际应用落地。

Method: 采用监督式χ²统计引导的二值化方法将连续变量转换为二元特征，使伯努利朴素贝叶斯（BNB）模型能够在保持完全透明性的同时处理连续医学数据，并配合交叉验证的泄露安全概率校准（Brier分数、校准截距/斜率、事后beta校准）。

Result: 在皮马印第安人糖尿病（AUC=0.800）、威斯康星乳腺癌（AUC=0.984）和心力衰竭预测（AUC=0.919）三个基准数据集上取得高性能，且概率校准质量得到改善。

Conclusion: 统计可解释框架能够在实现与复杂模型相当性能的同时，提供明确的临床决策规则和校准的风险估计，且推理过程仅需参考表和基础算术即可手工复现，支持可信赖、可泛化的医疗AI应用。

Abstract: Black-box models limit the adoption of artificial intelligence in medicine due to their lack of interpretability and reproducibility. We introduce a statistically grounded framework that provides fully interpretable, rule-based clinical classification using the Bernoulli Naïve Bayes (BNB) model. The method applies supervised $χ^2$-guided statistical binarization to continuous variables, identifying thresholds that maximize association with clinical outcomes within the training data. This transformation allows BNB to operate effectively on continuous medical data without sacrificing its inherent transparency. The approach was evaluated on three benchmark datasets, Pima Indians Diabetes, Wisconsin Breast Cancer, and Heart Failure Prediction, achieving area-under-the-curve (AUC) scores of 0.800 for the Pima analysis, 0.984 for Wisconsin Breast Cancer, and 0.919 for Heart Failure Prediction. In addition to discrimination, probabilistic reliability was assessed using leakage-safe cross-validated calibration analysis including Brier score, calibration intercept/slope, and post-hoc beta calibration, which improved probability calibration across datasets. These results suggest that a statistically interpretable framework can achieve performance comparable to more complex models while providing explicit, clinically meaningful decision rules and calibrated risk estimates. To illustrate this transparency concretely, a complete worked example demonstrates that model inference can be reproduced using only a reference table and basic arithmetic, without access to software or proprietary tools. This work offers a practical approach to supporting trustworthy and generalizable AI in real-world healthcare settings.

### [21] [Regularity-Aware Stochastic MGDA with Adaptive Conflict-Avoidant Update Direction Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15412)
*Chentong Huang,Lisha Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了随机多目标优化中多梯度下降算法的收敛性问题。发现冲突避免（CA）方向具有1/2-Hölder连续性且该指数不可改进，这导致标准随机MGDA的收敛速率次优。在额外正则条件下可提升至Lipschitz连续。据此提出MoRe方法，根据子问题正则性自适应切换CA方向更新与固定标量化权重更新，在非凸设定下将收敛率从Õ(T^{-1/4})提升至Õ(T^{-1/2})，同时保证逐次冲突避免，实验验证了多任务性能与理论收敛速率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机MGDA（SMG）在随机设置下收敛速率慢，主要原因是小批量采样引入梯度噪声，导致更新方向存在偏差，该偏差受CA方向连续性的控制。现有研究未能充分刻画CA方向的连续性及其对收敛速率的影响。

Method: 理论分析CA方向的连续性，证明其为1/2-Hölder连续且该指数不可改进；在额外正则条件下可提升为Lipschitz连续。提出MoRe方法：当子问题正则时利用Lipschitz连续性进行CA方向更新，否则切换为固定标量化权重更新。直觉上，梯度冲突大时用CA方向，否则用线性标量化。

Result: 理论上，在非凸设定下将收敛率从Õ(T^{-1/4})提升至Õ(T^{-1/2})，并建立了逐次冲突避免保证。实验验证了多任务性能与理论收敛速率的一致性。

Conclusion: MoRe方法通过自适应更新策略有效提升了随机多目标优化的收敛速度，理论分析与实验验证均支持其有效性。

Abstract: Multi-objective learning (MOL) aims to optimize multiple objectives simultaneously. The multi-gradient descent algorithm (MGDA) is a workhorse that iteratively updates along a common descent or conflict-avoidant (CA) direction across objectives. In stochastic settings, however, the vanilla stochastic MGDA method, SMG, lacks a fast convergence rate because mini-batch sampling introduces noise in the gradients. This causes bias in the update direction, which is controlled by the CA direction continuity. In this paper, we show that the CA direction is $1/2$-Holder continuous with respect to the Jacobian matrix, and the exponent $1/2$ cannot be improved in the worst case. This leads to a suboptimal convergence rate for vanilla stochastic MGDA in prior works. Nevertheless, under additional regularity conditions, we show this can be improved to Lipschitz continuity. Based on this insight, we propose a stochastic multi-objective regularity-aware (MoRe) method that exploits the Lipschitz continuity of the CA direction when the subproblem is regular, and switches to a fixed scalarization weight otherwise. Intuitively, the proposed algorithm employs CA direction update when the gradient conflict is large, and linear scalarization update otherwise. Theoretically, our method improves the convergence rate of SMG in the nonconvex setting from $\widetilde{\mathcal O}(T^{-1/4})$ to $\widetilde{\mathcal O}(T^{-1/2})$, where $\widetilde{\mathcal O}(\cdot)$ hides logarithmic factors. Meanwhile, we also establish the per-iterate conflict-avoidance guarantees. Empirically, experiments demonstrate its effectiveness in multi-task performance and verify convergence behavior consistent with the established theoretical rate.

</details>


### [22] [AI Trading: Evaluating Large Language Models for Technical Market Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15414)
*Geofrey Ntale*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代金融市场信息环境异构复杂，LLM作为新型工具展现出处理能力，但缺乏对其在技术分析领域系统性的横向比较评估，尤需填补通用模型与领域专用模型在量化指标上的对比空白。

Method: 构建包含K线模式识别、方向信号生成、模拟交易回测和财报理解四类任务的评估框架，采用夏普比率、最大回撤、索提诺比率、信息系数、F1分数和BLEU分数等多维量化指标，在模拟执行流水线上对五种LLM进行标准化对比。

Result: GPT-4 Turbo在通用模型中取得最高年化收益率和夏普比率；FinGPT凭借领域微调展现了具有竞争力的风险调整后收益；两者均超越被动型S&P 500基准。所有模型均存在数值幻觉、上下文窗口限制以及在横盘市场中的表现不一致等系统性失败模式。

Conclusion: LLM在AI交易系统中具有真实潜力，但稳健部署需要谨慎的任务分解、严格的回测协议和领域感知的微调策略。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have emerged as powerful tools for processing the heterogeneous information environments of modern financial markets. This paper presents a systematic, comparative evaluation of five prominent LLMs: GPT-4 Turbo, Claude 3 Opus, Gemini 1.5 Pro, Llama 3 70B, and the domain-specialized FinGPT, with respect to their capacity for technical market analysis. The evaluation spans four structured tasks: candlestick pattern recognition from OHLCV data, directional signal generation (BUY/SELL/HOLD), backtesting of signal quality through a simulated execution pipeline, and financial report comprehension. Our experimental framework employs rigorous quantitative metrics, including Sharpe ratio, maximum drawdown, Sortino ratio, information coefficient, F1-score, and BLEU score. Findings from simulated backtesting indicate that GPT-4 Turbo achieves the highest annualized return and Sharpe ratio among general-purpose models, while FinGPT demonstrates competitive risk-adjusted performance due to domain-specific fine-tuning. Both models outperform a passive S&P 500 benchmark under the tested conditions. The study identifies persistent failure modes across all evaluated models, including numerical hallucination, context-window limitations, and inconsistent performance in sideways market regimes. We conclude that while LLMs hold genuine promise within AI trading systems, robust deployment requires careful task decomposition, rigorous backtesting protocols, and domain-aware fine-tuning strategies.

</details>


### [23] [Diffusion models recover accurate mixture weights despite score function insensitivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15485)
*Andrew Dennehy,Ramchandran Muthukumar,Rebecca Willett,Nisha Chandramoorthy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过提出扩散分数敏感度指数（DSSI），解释了基于分数的生成模型虽能覆盖多模态分布的所有模式，却可能错误估计混合权重（即模式幅度）的表观矛盾。研究发现，扩散分数匹配（DSM）损失与混合权重估计误差之间存在量化关系，且中间噪声层的分数信息对权重恢复至关重要。在理论上证明了高斯混合模型中权重估计误差与DSM损失同阶，实验验证了噪声调度对敏感度及模式放大的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决基于分数的生成模型中一个矛盾现象：模型看似覆盖了目标多模态分布的所有模式，但无法正确学习各模式的相对幅度（混合权重）。作者希望通过理论分析揭示这一悖论的本质原因。

Method: 1. 将DSM损失与混合权重估计误差建立理论关联；2. 定义扩散分数敏感度指数（DSSI），衡量DSM损失相对于参数变化的变化量；3. 在高斯混合模型下证明权重估计误差与DSM损失同阶；4. 在基准数据分布上通过实验验证噪声调度对敏感度和模式恢复的影响。

Result: 1. 证明了混合权重估计误差与DSM损失在温和条件下同阶；2. 发现中间噪声层的分数信息对权重恢复起关键作用；3. 实验表明噪声调度选择可以降低扩散敏感度，从而影响模式放大现象；4. DSSI框架可推广到目标分布的任何定性参数估计。

Conclusion: 基于分数的生成模型中混合权重恢复精度可由DSSI量化预测，噪声调度是影响敏感度和模式放大的关键因素。该敏感度分析框架不仅限于混合权重，可推广至目标分布的其他定性参数。

Abstract: Score-based generative models exhibit a puzzling behavior: they often appear to cover all modes of a target multimodal distribution and yet may fail to learn the correct relative mode amplitudes, which can be interpreted as mixture weights. We resolve this apparent paradox by relating the diffusion score matching (DSM) loss to the error in estimating mixture weights from generated samples. We show that, even when the target score is insensitive to mixture weights, generated samples can recover the weights accurately if the scores at intermediate noise levels are informative about the weights. Accordingly, we define the diffusion score sensitivity index (DSSI) as the variation in the DSM loss relative to changes in a parameter. We then show that the DSSI governs the accuracy with which the parameter of the target distribution can be estimated from generated samples. For Gaussian mixtures in arbitrary dimensions, we prove that the mixture weight estimation errors are on the same order as the DSM loss under mild conditions. Empirically, we show the emergence of sensitivity during the noising process of benchmark data distributions under typical noise schedules, and that these sensitivity values predict how well a well-trained model recovers mixture weights. Furthermore, we show that the choice of noise schedule can reduce diffusion sensitivity, leading to mode amplification. Although we focus on mixture weights, the proposed sensitivity framework governs the recovery of any qualitative parameter of the target distribution.

</details>


### [24] [qZACH-ViT: Quantization-Aware Intrinsic Explanations with Recursive Attribution-Stabilized Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15421)

Abstract: Compact medical-image classifiers need efficiency and interpretable evidence, yet these goals are often addressed separately. We introduce qZACH-ViT, a quantization-aware extension of the zero-token (CLS-token-free), position-free ZACH-ViT backbone with recursive intrinsic patch-level class evidence. We also introduce Recursive Attribution-Stabilized Optimization (RASO), which norm-matches classification and attribution gradients and removes attribution components that conflict with classification. We evaluate four controlled conditions on seven MedMNIST datasets using 50 training images per class and ten fixed seeds, completing 280 runs. All 210 qZACH-ViT checkpoints are converted to executable mixed-precision ONNX INT8 graphs containing 16 signed INT8 MatMulInteger projections with INT32 accumulation. Across 964,920 source-to-INT8 test comparisons, prediction agreement is 99.9751\%, with a mean absolute primary-metric change of 0.000133 and a maximum of 0.004386. Across 3,600 matched intrinsic maps, mean cosine similarity is 0.999955, mean rank correlation is 0.9944, and mean top-10\% overlap is 0.9692. ONNX artifacts are 70.0\% smaller than source checkpoints and provide $1.41\times$ and $2.39\times$ end-to-end CPU speedups with one and four threads. RASO significantly reduces sufficiency error and improves input-noise stability over Adam with the same attribution loss, but does not dominate every predictive or explainable artificial intelligence (XAI) metric. These results establish qZACH-ViT as a deployable compact intrinsically explainable model and RASO as a targeted stability-oriented optimization procedure.

### [25] [Do Generative Models Keep Time? A Time-Aware Evaluation of Synthetic Sequential Tabular Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15606)
*Kiwan Kwon,Kangmin Kim,Hojin Lee,Yeseong Jung,Hyeongwoo Kong,Vamsi K. Potluru,Saerom Park,Yongjae Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于分类学引导的时间保真度评估协议，用于评估合成序列表格数据中时间动态的保真度。该协议根据数据的四个属性（时间表示、采样规律性、轨迹依赖性、模式链接）动态确定评估维度，包括时间戳有效性、横向结构、实体动态和时变关系结构，并在13个数据集上对8个生成模型进行了测试。结果显示，传统评估方法与时间评估方法的排名存在显著差异，且失败模式与模型架构相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的合成序列表格数据评估方法将记录汇集到静态分布中，无法检测到时间戳倒退、重复以及实体路径不真实等时间维度的错误，亟需一种能在时间轴本身测量时间保真度的评估协议。

Method: 提出分类学引导的评估协议：首先根据数据的四个属性（时间表示、采样规律性、轨迹依赖性、模式链接）对数据集进行分类，然后基于分类结果动态确定适用的评估维度，测量时间戳有效性、横向结构、实体动态和时变关系结构，并将效用和隐私评估从单行重构为轨迹级别。

Result: 在13个数据集、8个生成模型上的实验表明，传统评估与时间评估的排名结果存在显著分歧，且时间保真度失败模式与模型架构一致，而非随机出现。

Conclusion: 时间保真度必须在时间轴本身进行测量，而非从汇集记录分布中推断；评估协议应基于数据特性动态确定评估维度，而非固定预设。

Abstract: Synthetic sequential tabular data are increasingly used for privacy-preserving data sharing, yet a generator can reproduce every marginal and every foreign-key relationship while emitting timestamps that run backwards or repeat, and while sending entities along paths that no real entity followed. Conventional tabular evaluation, which pools records into static distributions, is blind to such failures. We present a taxonomy-guided evaluation protocol for temporal fidelity, in which the applicable measurements are determined by the data rather than fixed in advance. Each dataset is first characterized along four properties: how time is represented, whether observations are regularly sampled, whether trajectories are mutually dependent, and how the schema links entities to their histories. These properties determine which evaluation dimensions are meaningful. The protocol then measures timestamp validity, cross-sectional structure at aligned time points, within-entity dynamics, and time-varying relational structure, and recasts utility and privacy evaluation over trajectories rather than isolated rows. We apply the protocol to eight generative models across thirteen datasets spanning six domains. Rankings under conventional evaluation disagree substantially with those obtained under temporal evaluation, and the resulting failures are architecture-coherent rather than random. Temporal fidelity must therefore be measured on the time axis itself, rather than inferred from pooled record distributions.

### [27] [Neural Non-Equilibrium Hamiltonian Monte Carlo for Corrected Boltzmann Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15682)
*Moxian Qian*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出神经非平衡哈密顿蒙特卡洛（NHMC），一种可训练-校正的学习型哈密顿采样器。NHMC从可处理的基分布出发，学习朝向目标的随机哈密顿路径，训练后固定提议参数，利用非平衡功对生成的路径和端点构型进行统计校正。最小化平均功可降低路径空间KL散度并控制端点失配上界；评估时该量可用于路径自归一化重要性采样（path-SNIS）、估计归一化常数/自由能差，以及路径独立Metropolis-Hastings（path-IMH）的接受率。该框架还定义了共享桥往返Metropolis核，直接作用于构型并保持玻尔兹曼目标。在双势阱和有限体积格点φ⁴靶标上，当路径重叠足够时NHMC给出校正估计；重叠不足时，权重退化、低接受率和长自相关暴露提议失败。另报告了使用分子动力学先验和学习力路径提议的分子内坐标可行性研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从非归一化玻尔兹曼密度中采样需要能在全局范围内移动概率质量、同时保留足够路径概率信息以进行统计校正的提议机制。现有方法在平衡高维复杂分布时面临挑战。

Method: 提出NHMC方法：先训练学习随机哈密顿路径（从基分布到目标分布），训练后固定参数；再用非平衡功对生成路径和端点进行统计校正。使用前向-反向路径概率比定义的广义功，最小化其均值以降低路径空间KL散度；评估时该量用于path-SNIS、path-IMH和共享桥往返Metropolis核。

Result: 在双势阱和有限体积格点φ⁴靶标上验证：路径重叠足够时NHMC给出校正估计；重叠不足时权重退化、低接受率和长自相关暴露失败。另在分子内坐标任务中展示了可行性。

Conclusion: NHMC是一种结合学习与校正的哈密顿采样框架，通过非平衡功实现路径空间的统计校正，能有效处理玻尔兹曼分布采样问题，但性能依赖于路径重叠质量。

Abstract: Sampling from an unnormalized Boltzmann density requires proposals that move probability mass globally while retaining enough path-probability information for statistical correction. We introduce Neural Non-Equilibrium Hamiltonian Monte Carlo (NHMC), a train-then-correct learned Hamiltonian sampler. Starting from a tractable base distribution, NHMC learns stochastic Hamiltonian-style paths toward the target. Once training is complete, the learned proposal parameters are fixed; the proposal then generates complete paths and endpoint configurations, which are statistically corrected using the recorded non-equilibrium work. This dimensionless generalized work is determined by the probability ratio between the forward proposal path and a reverse reference path. During training, minimizing its mean reduces a path-space KL divergence and controls an upper bound on endpoint mismatch. During evaluation, the same quantity defines weights for self-normalized importance sampling on paths (path-SNIS), estimates normalizing constants or free-energy differences, and gives the acceptance ratio for path-space independent Metropolis-Hastings (path-IMH). The same forward-reverse laws also define a shared-bridge round-trip Metropolis kernel that acts directly on configurations and preserves the Boltzmann target. On double-well and finite-volume lattice $φ^4$ targets, the NHMC construction gives corrected estimates when path overlap is sufficient; when overlap is poor, weight degeneracy, low acceptance, and long autocorrelation expose proposal failure. We additionally report a molecular internal-coordinate feasibility study using an MD prior and learned-force path proposal.

Method: 提出ASK-NN（Asymmetric k-Nearest Neighbor）检验方法，基于有向k近邻图构建统计量：统计参考样本中那些在合并样本中的最近邻也属于参考样本的点数。该方法在置换零假设下具有精确的有限样本条件均值和方差，并建立了渐近正态性和一致性理论保证。计算高效且易于实现。

Abstract: Hallucinations and artificial text in LLM-generated outputs often appear as distributional deviations between prompt and response hidden-state distributions. Since prompts or retrieved contexts typically serve as reference samples and responses as query samples, with major differences in length, these asymmetries motivate the use of change test statistics that treat the two samples differently. We consider an asymmetric two-sample test ASK-NN based on the directed k-nearest-neighbor graph. Our statistic counts reference points whose nearest neighbor in the pooled sample is also a reference point. Under the permutation null, it admits an exact finite-sample conditional mean and variance; we further establish asymptotic normality and consistency under fixed alternatives. ASK-NN is computationally effective and easy to implement. Empirically, it is competitive with kernel and graph-based baselines on synthetic benchmarks, artificial-text detection, and LLM hallucination detection from token-level hidden states.

### [29] [Stochastic Reset Pathfinding: Path-Level Regret for Cascading Bandits over Graph Paths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15440)
*Guni Sharon,Wei Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出随机重置寻径（SRP）问题，将其建模为组合级联赌博机（CCB）框架，提出Log-Dijkstra元算法（含PathUCB和PathTS两种实例化），为PathUCB建立了路径级遗憾界，并通过实验验证了算法性能，同时指出PathTS存在对抗性失效案例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子中继网络中的纠缠分发、闪电网络中的支付路由、不可靠mesh网络中的投递等现实场景中，路径在执行过程中可能发生边失败并将代理重置回起点，现有模型未能充分刻画这种全局重置结构及其带来的开环最优策略特性。

Method: 将SRP形式化为一个在已知有向图上、边成功概率未知且平稳的逐情节学习问题；证明全局重置结构使最优策略为开环策略，从而归入CCB框架；提出Log-Dijkstra元算法，使用UCB（PathUCB）和Thompson采样（PathTS）两种实例化；为PathUCB导出路径级遗憾界，通过每条子优路径的复杂度C(π)（结合每条边的前缀与后缀可靠性）来分解遗憾。

Result: PathUCB的路径级遗憾界比边级CCB界在具有多项式条源-目标路径的结构化图上更具信息性；在量子网络、分层DAG、网格世界和Erdos-Renyi图上的实验支持理论，PathTS在大多数测试场景中取得最佳经验性能；构造的对抗性实例显示PathTS不收敛，与组合TS在乘性奖励问题上的已知指数障碍一致。

Conclusion: 推荐PathTS作为实际默认算法，同时需注意存在对抗性实例使其失效。

Abstract: We introduce Stochastic Reset Pathfinding (SRP), an episodic learning problem on a known directed graph with unknown stationary edge success probabilities. In each episode, the agent commits to a source-to-goal path, and any edge failure during execution resets it to the source. SRP captures settings such as entanglement distribution in quantum repeater networks, payment routing on the Lightning Network, and delivery in unreliable mesh networks. We show that the global-reset structure makes the optimal policy open-loop, placing SRP within the combinatorial cascading bandit (CCB) framework. We propose a Log-Dijkstra meta-algorithm with UCB (PathUCB) and Thompson Sampling (PathTS) instantiations. Our main technical result is a path-level regret bound for PathUCB that decomposes regret over suboptimal paths via a per-path complexity C(pi) combining each edge's prefix and suffix reliability. The bound is complementary to the edge-level CCB bound and more informative on structured graphs with polynomially many source-to-goal paths. Experiments on quantum-network, layered-DAG, grid-world, and Erdos-Renyi domains support the theory and show that PathTS typically achieves the best empirical performance among the algorithms tested. We then exhibit an adversarial instance on which PathTS fails to converge, consistent with a known exponential obstruction for combinatorial Thompson Sampling on multiplicative-reward problems. We recommend PathTS as the practical default while cautioning that adversarial instances exist.

### [30] [Who Became Financially Vulnerable After COVID-19? A Population-Level Machine Learning Analysis Using MEPS Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15446)
*Alexey Kresin,Zien Cheng,Ammar Ahad,Ebiyomare Kelvin,Manish Sivaratri,Prabhjeet Singh,Omar Aljawfi,Olabisi Ojo,Nawar Shara*

TL;DR: 本研究利用2019年和2021年MEPS数据，结合逻辑回归与随机森林、梯度提升等机器学习模型，分析了COVID-19大流行前后美国医疗财务脆弱性的变化。结果显示，贫困状况、保险覆盖和处方药支出是关键预测因素；尽管2021年部分脆弱群体负担加重，但大流行前后脆弱性的主要预测因子保持相对稳定，模型在时间泛化中表现稳健。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 美国医疗费用负担持续受到关注，COVID-19大流行可能加剧了这一状况。本研究旨在评估大流行前后美国人群在医疗财务脆弱性方面的变化，特别是不同人口和社会经济群体之间的差异，以揭示大流行对医疗经济负担的冲击程度。

Method: 使用2019年和2021年医疗支出小组调查（MEPS）数据，将高财务负担定义为自付医疗支出超过家庭收入的10%。采用调查加权亚组分析获取全国代表性估计；同时构建可解释的逻辑回归（估计调整后优势比）与随机森林、梯度提升等机器学习模型进行预测性能评估。通过时间泛化测试评估基于大流行前数据训练的模型对大流行后数据的预测能力。

Result: 财务脆弱性与贫困状况、保险覆盖和处方药支出显著相关。亚组分析显示不同人群间存在持续的不平等，2021年部分脆弱群体的负担有所增加。然而，基于大流行前数据训练的模型在应用于大流行后数据时，预测性能仅出现适度下降，表明医疗财务脆弱性的主要预测因子在时间上保持相对稳定。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了COVID-19期间美国医疗财务脆弱性的人群水平评估，展示了将可解释统计建模与机器学习相结合在人口健康研究中的价值。研究结果可为未来人口健康监测、风险分层和旨在减少医疗经济障碍的政策研究提供支持。

Abstract: The cost of healthcare remains a concern in the United States and may have been influenced by disruptions associated with the COVID-19 pandemic. This study examines healthcare financial vulnerability before and after the pandemic using Medical Expenditure Panel Survey (MEPS) data from 2019 and 2021. High financial burden was defined as out-of-pocket healthcare expenditures exceeding 10% of family income. Survey-weighted subgroup analyses were performed to obtain nationally representative estimates across demographic and socioeconomic groups.
  Descriptive analyses were complemented by interpretable logistic regression and machine learning models. Logistic regression was used to estimate adjusted odds ratios, while random forest and gradient boosting models were used to evaluate predictive performance. Temporal generalization assessed whether models trained on pre-pandemic data remained predictive when applied to post-pandemic observations.
  Financial vulnerability was strongly associated with poverty status, insurance coverage, and prescription drug spending. Subgroup analyses indicated persistent disparities across population groups, with some evidence of increased burden among vulnerable populations in 2021. Despite these differences, models trained on pre-pandemic data exhibited only modest reductions in predictive performance when evaluated on post-pandemic data, suggesting that the principal predictors of healthcare financial vulnerability remained relatively stable over time.
  These findings provide a population-level assessment of healthcare financial vulnerability during the COVID-19 period and demonstrate the value of combining interpretable statistical modeling with machine learning for population health research. The results may support future population health surveillance, risk stratification, and healthcare policy research aimed at reducing financial barriers to care.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Recent research in clinical machine learning, focusing on outcome predictions in intensive care unit (ICU), has shifted from bespoke supervised models to foundation models, utilising modern representation learning methods. ### [32] [Relevant and Irrelevant: A Renormalization Group Analysis of Transformer Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15449)
*Parviz Haggi-Mani,Irina Rish*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文利用威尔逊重整化群理论，将Transformer的注意力机制视为对训练好的MLP残差流固定点的微扰，发现注意力是否相关（relevant）取决于数据生成过程的频谱结构：长程相关数据下注意力驱动表示空间的相变（有效秩跃升、损失缺口闭合），短程相关下则无关（收敛于MLP相同固定点）。首层首个注意力头贡献了超过4倍其他头的表示偏移，且注意力对慢模式的选择性保留呈现出动态范围反转。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点将注意力机制视为Transformer的核心组件，但对其在表示空间中究竟扮演什么角色缺乏理论理解。作者希望从RG理论视角，将注意力视为对MLP残差流固定点的微扰，回答"注意力是否以及何时是相关算子"这一根本问题。

Method: 推导了固定点偏移公式，得到四个可检验预测（固定点几何、有效秩分布、层特异性、微扰衰减谱），并在合成马尔可夫链数据（控制相关长度）上进行实验验证。

Result: （1）长程相关下注意力相关：闭合MLP无法弥补的损失缺口，驱动表示空间相变（有效秩跃升至超过输入维度）；（2）短程相关下注意力无关：收敛于MLP相同固定点；（3）L0H0贡献超过4倍其他头的表示偏移；（4）长程下注意力选择性保留慢模式（衰减长度动态范围5.4倍 vs MLP的1.3倍），短程下无选择性。

Conclusion: 注意力的相关性不是架构的固有属性，而是数据生成过程的频谱结构决定的。一阶RG微扰框架能够预测性地解释这种差异。

Abstract: Using the language of Wilsonian renormalization group theory (RG), we treat the Transformer's attention mechanism as a perturbation of the trained MLP residual-stack fixed point and ask whether it constitutes a relevant, marginal, or irrelevant operator. We derive a fixed-point shift formula and obtain four testable predictions for the fixed-point geometry, effective rank profile, layer specificity, and perturbation decay spectrum. Testing these on synthetic Markov chain sequences with controlled correlation length, we find: (1) For large chains(long correlation), attention is strongly relevant: it closes a residual loss gap the MLP cannot bridge and drives a phase transition in representation space, with effective rank jumping above input dimensionality at layer 1 and stabilizing at a high-dimensional plateau. (2) For short chains(short correlation), attention is irrelevant: the Transformer converges to the same loss and fixed-point geometry as the MLP, though it contracts perturbations faster. (3) The transition is dominated by the first-layer head (L0H0), which accounts for more than 4 times the representational shift of any subsequent head, consistent with the prediction that the relevant operator acts before the MLP begins integrating out positional variation. (4) Perturbation decay experiments reveal a regime reversal: in the long correlation regime the Transformer selectively preserves slow Markov modes (5.4 times the dynamic range in decay length vs. 1.3 times for the MLP); in the short correlation regime it suppresses all modes faster than the MLP, with no spectral selectivity. Together, these results show that the relevance of attention is not a property of the architecture but of the spectral structure of the data-generating process, and that a first-order RG perturbation framework provides a predictive account of that difference.

</details>


### [33] [Looped Latent Attention: Cross-Loop KV Compression for Looped Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15456)
*James O' Neill,Fergal Reid*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出循环潜在注意力(LLA)，一种针对循环权重共享Transformer的后训练缓存编解码器。通过分析发现循环索引的K/V缓存具有低秩结构，LLA存储紧凑的K/V潜在向量，仅在注意力读取时重建循环特定的K/V向量。对比MLA、跨层共享、KV量化和最终循环重用等方法，LLA在相同缓存预算下表现更优。在H200上实现21.3倍压缩，4k上下文下批量容量从32提升到768序列。长数学推理中，MATH-500从0.43提升至0.66。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 循环权重共享Transformer虽然减少了参数，但解码时仍为每个循环步存储独立的K/V缓存，导致内存开销大。作者发现循环索引的缓存具有高度结构化特性：固定token、层和头时，K/V向量在循环间呈短低秩轨迹。利用这一特性设计更高效的缓存压缩方法。

Method: 提出Looped Latent Attention (LLA)，一种后训练缓存编解码器。默认使用每头编解码器压缩循环维度（per-head LLA），LLA-2D则将头也折叠进一个潜在向量实现极限压缩。编解码器通过教师激活的SVD初始化，并使用KL散度和注意力输出蒸馏进行微调。

Result: 在相同缓存预算下，per-head LLA优于MLA、跨层共享、KV量化和最终循环重用。Ouro-1.4B在4k上下文下实现21.3倍压缩，批量容量从32提升到768序列。Ouro-2.6B-Thinking和Huginn-3.5B上SVD编解码器在32倍压缩下几乎无损。长数学推理中，MATH-500从0.43提升至0.66，减少无回答生成。

Conclusion: 循环缓存是低秩的，但不能安全地折叠为单一状态。轴优势（循环轴vs头轴/层轴）在不同模型间具有迁移性。缓存缩减是精确的（无损解码），且通过学生生成前缀的在线策略微调可显著提升长数学推理性能。

Abstract: Looped, weight-tied Transformers reduce parameters by reusing a block, but decoding still stores a separate K/V cache for every recurrence step. We show that this loop-indexed cache is highly structured. For a fixed token, layer and head, K/V vectors trace a short low-rank trajectory across loops, while the head and layer axes remain much flatter. We introduce Looped Latent Attention (LLA), a post-training cache codec that stores compact K and V latents and reconstructs loop-specific K/V vectors only when attention reads them. The default per-head codec compresses recurrence, while LLA-2D also folds heads into one latent for the extreme-compression regime. The codec is initialized from SVD of teacher activations and refined with KL and attention-output distillation. At matched cache budget, per-head LLA outperforms head-axis MLA, cross-layer sharing, KV quantization and final-loop reuse, showing that the recurrent cache is low-rank but not safely collapsible to a single state. The same axis advantage holds on Ouro-2.6B-Thinking and transfers to Huginn-3.5B, where an SVD codec remains near-lossless to 32x in decoder-independent evaluation. The cache reduction is exact. On one H200, the latent-store path increases measured Ouro-1.4B batch capacity at 4k context from 32 to 768 sequences at 21.3x compression. For long math rollouts, on-policy refinement on student-generated prefixes raises MATH-500 at 4x from 0.43 to 0.66 and reduces no-answer generations.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统CMDP基于期望累积代价，无法捕捉单次大违规带来的灾难性后果；峰值代价约束MDP的对偶性质尚不清晰，且存在仿真到现实环境的动力学不匹配问题。

Method: 1) 证明峰值代价约束MDP可能存在非零对偶间隙；2) 提出基于积分概率度量的鲁棒价值估计方法；3) 构建替代优化框架，通过合理超参数选择使替代解在约束违反不超过ε的前提下达到与原始问题相同的鲁棒奖励值。

Conclusion: 峰值代价约束MDP存在对偶间隙问题，所提出的鲁棒替代优化框架可有效解决该问题，在安全关键应用中具有实用价值。

Abstract: We study robust peak-cost constrained reinforcement learning (RP-CRL), where the objective is to maximize expected reward while controlling the maximum cost encountered along a trajectory. This setting is motivated by safety-critical applications in which a single large violation can be catastrophic and therefore cannot be adequately captured by the standard CMDP framework based on expected cumulative cost. Existing reachability-constrained RL methods adopt Lagrangian-based approaches, yet the underlying duality properties of peak-cost constrained MDPs remain unclear. We show that, unlike standard CMDPs, peak-cost constrained MDPs may not admit zero duality gap. We further consider a robust formulation to address simulator-to-real-world mismatch in the transition dynamics. To solve this problem, we develop a surrogate optimization framework and a robust value estimation method based on integral probability metrics. We prove that, with appropriate hyperparameter choices, the surrogate solution attains the same robust reward value as the original problem while violating the constraint by at most epsilon. Experiments show that the proposed method effectively enforces safety under dynamics perturbations while retaining strong reward performance.

### [35] [ADS-C: Antidistillation Sampling for Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15467)
*Khawaja Abaid Ullah,Mohammad Javad Khojasteh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文提出ADS-C，一种针对分类任务的抗蒸馏防御方法，通过闭式逐输入边际预算施加扰动，在零教师准确率损失下有效防御知识蒸馏攻击。在CIFAR-10/100和Tiny-ImageNet上，学生准确率分别下降29.6、17.4和13.3个百分点，而硬标签攻击者毫无收获。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 知识蒸馏使攻击者能够通过查询预测接口并训练替代模型来复制专有分类器。现有针对大语言模型的抗蒸馏采样方法（反蒸馏采样）尚未被研究如何迁移到分类任务，且直接迁移存在缺陷。

Method: 1. 将大语言模型的抗蒸馏采样方法适配到分类任务，发现其行为由教师置信度边际分布决定。2. 分析直接迁移存在的"惰性窗口"现象和相变行为。3. 提出ADS-C方法，在闭式逐输入边际预算下施加扰动，严格保留每个top-1预测，实现零教师准确率损失。

Result: 在CIFAR-100上学生准确率下降17.4个百分点，CIFAR-10下降29.6，Tiny-ImageNet下降13.3。同等学生退化程度下，未修改防御需要牺牲27.5、32.9和22.2的教师准确率。硬标签攻击者零收益，软输出训练的学生比硬标签基线还低29.7个百分点。

Conclusion: ADS-C是首个在分类任务中实现零效用成本（即教师准确率完全不变）的抗蒸馏防御方法，不仅消除了蒸馏激励，还逆转了激励方向——使蒸馏软概率比仅用硬标签更差。

Abstract: Knowledge distillation enables an adversary to replicate a proprietary classifier by querying its prediction interface and training a surrogate on the returned probability vectors. Antidistillation sampling, proposed for large language models, counters this threat with an input-dependent, gradient-directed perturbation of the served distribution; its transfer to classification has not been studied. Adapting the defense to classification, we show its behavior is governed by the distribution of the teacher's per-input confidence margins. Because well-trained classifiers are severely overconfident, the direct transfer exhibits an inert window: below a closed-form-predictable threshold, it affects neither attacker nor defender; beyond it, the defense undergoes a phase transition and degrades the teacher faster than the attacker's student. Temperature softening rescales the transition in closed form, and every temperature configuration lies on the same unfavorable trade-off curve. Our method, ADS-C, composes the perturbation under a closed-form, per-input margin budget that provably preserves every served top-1 prediction, so the defended teacher's accuracy equals the undefended teacher's identically. Under this guarantee the distilled student still loses 17.4 percentage points on CIFAR-100, 29.6 on CIFAR-10, and 13.3 on Tiny-ImageNet; matching this degradation with the unmodified defense costs 27.5, 32.9, and 22.2 points of teacher accuracy. Because served labels are unchanged, a hard-label attacker gains nothing, while the defended soft output trains a student up to 29.7 points below that floor: the incentive to distill served probabilities is not merely removed but reversed. To our knowledge, ADS-C is the first antidistillation defense for classification whose utility cost is exactly zero.

</details>

Abstract: Sleep apnea diagnosis via polysomnography remains resource intensive and relies on time consuming manual data analysis and scoring. Recent work has demonstrated that central nervous system effects of sleep apnea events can be detected through electroencephalogram (EEG) signals. However, most work uses a single feature type on various datasets combined with different classification algorithms. In this work, we present a comprehensive comparison of deep learning architectures and feature representations for automated sleep apnea detection from multichannel EEG on a single dataset of pediatric subjects. We evaluate Vision Transformers and Graph Attention Networks across distinct signal representations: raw temporal signals, short-time Fourier transform spectrograms, coherence based graphs, and two topological data analysis (TDA) derived features. Using age and sex matching of our train and test sets, we train on 2410 pediatric subjects and test on 575 pediatric subjects. We achieve a best test AUC of 0.750 using a vision transformer based model trained on TDA features. Stratified analysis across patient demographics (age, sex, AHI severity) and sleep stages (N1, N2, N3, REM) reveals significant performance variation. Our results demonstrate the feasibility of EEG based automated OSA screening while highlighting essential challenges for clinical deployment.

### [37] [Inpainting Insights: Elevating Visual XAI with Photorealistic Perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15482)
*Josef Lindl,Mariana Chaves,Damien Garreau*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对LIME等基于扰动的可解释性方法在图像上生成不真实样本的问题，提出使用生成式图像修复技术替代传统扰动方式，产生更符合数据分布的光照真实扰动，从而提升解释质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 生成式修复产生的扰动样本更贴合原始数据分布，减少了分布外样本和伪影问题，提升了解释质量。

Conclusion: 生成式图像修复能有效改进基于扰动的XAI方法，使图像解释更可靠、更真实。

Abstract: The increasing complexity of state-of-the-art machine learning models has made their behavior progressively harder to interpret, spurring rapid advancements in the field of eXplainable Artificial Intelligence (XAI). Among many methods proposed, perturbation-based approaches play a major role. By systematically altering (perturbing) input features, these approaches measure the impact on the model's predictions. For image data, traditional perturbation techniques, often involve replacing pixel values e.g., with a pre-defined color. However, such approaches, but also more refined deterministic techniques, generate unrealistic out-of-distribution samples and often leave visible artifacts, which can mislead the model and compromise explanation quality. In this work, we adjust LIME, a widely used perturbation-based method, to demonstrate how generative inpainting can improve perturbation-based explanations for images. We achieve photorealistic perturbed samples that align better with the original data distribution and enhance explanation quality.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统强化学习算法在高维非线性动力系统中样本效率低下，需要大量环境交互，且受限于探索-利用困境导致的维度灾难，难以应用于具有密集传感器和执行器的复杂系统。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has recently emerged as a promising feedback control strategy for nonlinear and complex dynamical systems. However, RL algorithms are sample inefficient and require a large number of interaction with the environment to synthesize optimal control strategies. Consequently, applications of RL are typically limited to sparse sensors and actuators due to the curse of dimensionality entailed by the exploration-exploitation dilemma in high-dimensional spaces. In this work, we bridge RL and traditional optimal control for dynamical system with a novel Physics-EnhAnced Reinforcement Learning (PEARL) paradigm tailored to the control of high-dimensional and parametric dynamical systems, exploiting the differentibility of their dynamics. Specifically, PEARL employs an actor-adjoint algorithm that leverages automatic differentiation to compute policy gradients over short horizons and adjoint-based sensitivities of future returns approximated via neural networks, significantly reducing the number of environment interactions, while mitigating long-term gradient instabilities. Through two challenging parametric navigation problems in unsteady flows, we show that PEARL (i) effectively exploits differentiable environments to outperform state-of-the-art RL algorithms, (ii) is sample efficient, thanks to the physics-guided policy learning, (iii) generalizes across multiple scenarios, which is crucial when dealing with parametric systems, and (iv) enables scaling RL to high-dimensional state and action spaces, without requiring low-dimensional state representations or multi-agent strategies.

Method: 采用张量积B样条对未知场进行直接参数化，将可训练控制系数作为学习参数；保留残差训练范式以匹配物理信息神经网络（PINNs）的损失函数；通过固定边界控制系数实现强约束边界条件。

Abstract: This work introduces Physics-Informed Splines (PI-Splines), a structured spline-based architecture for physics-informed learning. Instead of representing the solution of a differential equation with a neural network, PI-Splines directly parametrize the unknown field through a tensor-product B-spline expansion with trainable control coefficients. This formulation preserves the residual-based training paradigm of Physics-Informed Neural Networks while providing compact support, explicit smoothness control, analytical derivatives, and a direct geometric interpretation of the trainable parameters. When compatible with the spline representation, boundary conditions can be imposed strongly by fixing suitable boundary control coefficients. The proposed method is evaluated on several benchmark problems of increasing difficulty and compared with standard physics-informed frameworks under matched governing equations, collocation sets, loss terms, and optimization procedures, so as to isolate the effect of the approximation architecture. Numerical experiments show that PI-Splines provide a competitive and stable alternative to neural physics-informed architectures, particularly in settings where structured representations, locality, and parameter efficiency are desirable.

The proposed approach detects and corrects weight faults using distance-aware correction rules, eliminating the need for retraining or architectural modification. The effectiveness of the proposed method in terms of the capability of tolerating hardware faults has been evaluated through performing fault injection at different Bit Error Rates (BERs).

### [42] [Cache-Aware Prompt Compression:A Two-Tier Cost Model for LLM API Caching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15516)
*Yan Song*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种缓存感知的提示压缩方法（CAPC），通过结合查询无关压缩与缓存控制，在真实生产环境中比传统查询感知压缩更便宜且质量几乎无损。实验表明，在Anthropic Sonnet API上，CAPC在LongBench-v2所有配置中成本最低，在三个生产工作负载上均优于缓存优先和查询感知压缩策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有提示压缩文献默认使用查询感知压缩，这会破坏前缀缓存（每次调用生成不同的压缩前缀，导致缓存失效）。然而，生产中同时使用提示缓存和压缩两种低成本手段，但二者存在根本冲突。作者希望量化这种冲突并寻找最优策略。

Method: 1. 实证测量Anthropic Sonnet 4.6 API的缓存命中率，发现其双层架构（hot tier冷热阈值约3500 tokens）。2. 建立成本模型预测查询感知压缩与缓存的交叉点。3. 提出CAPC：查询无关压缩 + 显式缓存控制 + 层级保留比率约束（防止过度压缩将前缀推入hot tier）。4. 在LongBench-v2、企业工具助手、知识图谱RAG流水线、tau-bench零售基准上验证。

Result: Sonnet缓存远非理想（ρ≈0.83而非1.0）；在真实ρ下，查询感知压缩在压缩比r≥6时击败朴素缓存。CAPC在LongBench-v2上16/16配置最便宜，平均比缓存优先节省49%，比查询感知压缩节省64%，比原始节省90%，质量损失≤0.05。企业助手实现51.7%成本降低（r=3）；FastAPI上9.3倍优于全缓存，httpx上2.4倍；tau-bench上CAPC奖励与原始完全相同（36/50, p=1.00），而查询感知压缩成本增加40.1%。

Conclusion: 查询感知压缩在生产中因破坏缓存可能导致负收益（负ROI），CAPC通过缓存感知设计实现了最低成本且不牺牲质量，是当前生产LLM部署中性价比最优的提示压缩策略。

Abstract: Production LLM deployments combine two cost-reduction primitives: prompt caching (a discounted rate for re-used token prefixes) and prompt compression (fewer tokens sent). The compression literature has standardized on query-aware methods that produce a different compressed prefix per query, mechanically invalidating the prefix-strict cache on every call. We characterize this cost empirically on Anthropic's Sonnet 4.6 API and find caching is far from the rho=1.0 ideal the literature assumes: Sonnet's cache has a two-tier architecture with a sharp threshold near 3,500 tokens, below which the hit rate plateaus at rho~0.83 across 30-call sessions. Our cost model predicts, and experiments confirm, that under realistic rho, query-aware compression beats naive caching at high compression ratios (r>=6). We propose Cache-Aware Prompt Compression (CAPC), pairing query-agnostic compression with explicit cache_control plus a tier-preserving ratio bound that prevents over-compression from pushing the cached prefix into the hot tier. CAPC is the cheapest strategy in 16/16 configurations on LongBench-v2, with mean savings of 49% over cache-only, 64% over query-aware compression, and 90% over vanilla, at quality within 0.05 of the uncompressed baseline. We validate CAPC on three production workloads: an enterprise tool-using assistant with a 94k-token schema prefix (51.7% cost reduction at r=3); a graphify knowledge-graph RAG pipeline across two codebases (9.3x vs cache-all on FastAPI, 2.4x on httpx); and the public tau-bench retail benchmark (50 tasks), where CAPC is the cheapest of four strategies with reward exactly equal to vanilla (both 36/50, p=1.00) while query-aware compression is the most expensive at +40.1% over vanilla -- the first production confirmation of the crossover model's negative-ROI prediction on a public benchmark.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将框架表示为智能体循环的提示级规范，利用自身修订历史中的成对反馈进行迭代优化，称为递归式框架自我改进（RHI）。
