<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: HIT中速度环流的重要统计性质已被揭示，但尚不清楚这些性质在其他类型湍流中是否保持或改变。鉴于小尺度结构在HIT环流涨落中的主导作用，本文旨在探究它们在Rayleigh-Bénard对流这一非均匀、各向异性湍流中的相关性。

Method: 采用直接数值模拟（DNS）方法，对Rayleigh数10^9、Prandtl数O(1)的Rayleigh-Bénard对流进行数值模拟，分析热边界层内及远离边界层区域的环流统计特性，包括涡旋分布、核心纵横比、环流概率分布函数及面积法则的适用性。

Result: 1) 热边界层内基本涡旋分布与温度场强相关，核心纵横比统计显著改变；2) 平行于壁面的平面轮廓环流PDF与HIT相似，面积法则仍满足，但在距壁面数个TBL厚度处可能存在过渡区域；3) 远离边界层区域统计行为回归HIT特征，小尺度涡管间歇性分布由能量耗散场主导。

Conclusion: 尽管热边界层内局部结构受热效应显著改变，但环流的整体统计特性（尤其是面积法则）在Rayleigh-Bénard对流中仍保持与HIT高度相似，表明这些环流统计规律具有一定普适性；仅在边界层附近存在可能的过渡区，需进一步研究。

Abstract: Important statistical properties of velocity circulation in homogeneous isotropic turbulence (HIT) have been unveiled in recent years, raising the question of whether they persist, or are modified, in other classes of turbulent flows. Motivated by the dominant role of small-scale structures in the circulation fluctuations of HIT, we investigate their relevance in direct numerical simulations of Rayleigh-Bénard convection at a Rayleigh number of $10^9$ and Prandtl number of $O(1)$. Within the thermal boundary layer (TBL), the distribution of elementary vortices is found to be strongly correlated with the temperature field, while the statistics of their core aspect ratios is significantly altered. Additionally, the probability distribution functions of circulation, computed for planar contours which are parallel to the walls, display salient features closely akin to those observed in HIT, with the {\it Area Rule} (a connection between circulation statistics and minimal surfaces) remaining particularly well satisfied -- except for a possible transitional region at a distance of a few TBL thicknesses. Away from the TBL, as expected, the overall statistical behavior of these structures likewise resembles that of HIT, where the intermittent spatial distribution of small vortex tubes is instead determined by the energy dissipation field.

</details>


### [91] [Unified Deflection Estimation and Error Analysis for Background-Oriented Schlieren](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15567)
*Jiawei Li,Xiang Li,Chong Pan,Yuan Xiong*

TL;DR: 本文基于几何光学建立了统一的背景纹影（BOS）偏折估计框架，将二维和三维主流方法纳入同一数学结构，揭示了四种关键近似假设（薄相位物体、均匀边界折射率、近轴近似、偏折矢量与光轴垂直）的层级关系，并通过一维啁啾信号和二维DNS湍流场的非线性光线追踪验证了各方法的误差特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维BOS使用直观的偏折角，而三维层析BOS依赖严格的偏折矢量，两种描述独立发展，缺乏统一框架来桥接其假设并量化系统误差。

Method: 基于几何光学推导统一的偏折估计框架，解构四种关键假设，导出二维和三维空间中的统一偏折表达式，并使用一维啁啾信号和二维DNS湍流场结合非线性光线追踪进行验证。

Result: 建立了统一的BOS偏折估计框架，揭示了各主流方法对应的近似假设层级，定量表征并解析解释了不同边界条件下各方法的偏折估计误差。

Conclusion: 该工作为评估和提升定量BOS诊断的准确性提供了理论工具包。

Abstract: Background-Oriented Schlieren (BOS) has become a versatile quantitative diagnostic for density-varying flows, in which estimating the light-ray deflection from the measured displacement is the essential step linking the recorded images to the underlying refractive-index field. Two-dimensional BOS traditionally treats this through the intuitive deflection angle, whereas three-dimensional tomographic BOS relies on the rigorous deflection vector derived from the ray equation. These descriptions have evolved largely independently, and the assumptions bridging them, together with the systematic errors they introduce, have not been examined in a unified manner. Based on geometric optics, this study establishes a unified deflection estimation framework that reconciles the mainstream two- and three-dimensional methods into a single mathematical structure and exposes the hierarchy of approximations underlying each. By deconstructing four key assumptions, namely the thin phase object, the uniform boundary refractive index, the paraxial approximation, and the perpendicularity between the deflection vector and the optical axis, we derive rigorous unified deflection expressions in both two- and three-dimensional space and categorize the mainstream methods accordingly. Using phase objects constructed from one-dimensional chirp signals and two-dimensional turbulent fields from Direct Numerical Simulation, combined with high-fidelity nonlinear ray tracing as the ground truth, we quantitatively characterize and analytically interpret the deflection estimation error of each method under both uniform and non-uniform refractive-index boundary conditions. This work provides a theoretical toolkit for assessing and enhancing the accuracy of quantitative BOS diagnostics.

### [92] [Statistical State Dynamics Eigenmodes and Equilibria Form the Structural Basis of Couette Turbulence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15842)
*Brian F. Farrell,Petros J. Ioannou*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文通过二阶统计态动力学（SSD）框架，证明了宽通道Couette湍流中的滚流条带结构（RSS）源于模态不稳定性并平衡为吸引子固定点，揭示了其解析基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Navier-Stokes方程在速度变量下无法解析描述宽通道Couette湍流中稳态滚流条带结构（RSS）的线性不稳定性或稳定平衡态，导致该湍流状态的解析基础模糊不清。

Method: 采用二阶统计态动力学（SSD）方法，在统计状态空间中分析Couette湍流的固定点状态，识别模态RSS不稳定性及平衡过程。

Result: 发现SSD框架下存在一个固定点，该固定点源于模态RSS不稳定性，并在展向波数3处平衡为精确的吸引子RSS；该固定点由秩1流向平均流及其轭中性本征模态对构成，通过滚流对流而非粘性正则化，形成秩2涨落协方差。宽通道Couette湍流表现为该固定点RSS单胞的展向铺砌。

Conclusion: 二阶统计态动力学为宽通道Couette湍流中滚流条带结构的自维持机制提供了解析的理论基础，弥补了传统NS方程视角下的缺失。

Abstract: Wide channel Couette (WCC) turbulence consists primarily of steady roll streak structures (RSS) maintained by a self-sustaining process, yet the Navier Stokes equations in velocity variables admit no linear RSS instability or stable equilibrium, leaving the WCC turbulent state's analytical basis obscure. We show that in a second order statistical state dynamics (SSD) a fixed-point state of Couette turbulence arises from a modal RSS instability and equilibrates as an exact, attracting RSS at spanwise wavenumber 3. This fixed point comprises a rank-1 streamwise mean flow and a conjugate pair of neutral eigenmodes, regularized by roll advection rather than viscosity, forming a rank-2 fluctuation covariance. WCC turbulence arises as a spanwise tiling by this fixed-point RSS unit cell.

### [93] [Vortex formation around islands in random waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15938)
*Alex J. Vernon,Junyi Ye,Wenzhe Liu,Lei Shi,Konstantin Y. Bliokh*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该论文研究了二维随机波场中岛屿周围涡旋的统计理论，揭示了在旋转和非旋转系统中岛屿边缘涡旋出现的高概率（分别接近50%和100%），解释了特定大小（约特征波长的0.1倍）海洋岛屿周围潮汐涡旋的形成机制，并建立了缺陷诱导高强涡旋的普适原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已在M2海洋潮汐中观测到新西兰、马达加斯加、冰岛等地岛屿周围的涡旋现象，但控制其出现条件一直不清楚。本文旨在揭示随机二维波场中岛屿周围涡旋的形成条件和统计规律。

Method: 发展了随机二维波场（含/不含科里奥利效应）中岛屿周围涡旋的统计理论，并通过实验验证。计算了不同拓扑荷涡旋的概率作为岛屿尺寸和科里奥利参数的函数。

Result: 非旋转系统中岛屿边缘涡旋出现概率接近50%，旋转系统中接近100%；亚波长尺寸的岛屿在广泛参数范围内显著增强涡旋形成；特定大小（~0.1特征波长）的海洋岛屿对应潮汐涡旋的形成条件。

Conclusion: 建立了岛屿诱导涡旋形成的通用机制，解释了海洋潮汐涡旋的观测现象，并表明该机制可推广至水波、纳米光子结构等多种波系统，用于产生局域高强涡旋。

Abstract: Wave vortices are fundamental topological features of interference fields, occurring at nodal points where the wave amplitude vanishes. A distinct class of vortices can instead form around it islands or `holes' in two-dimensional wavefields, where the wave intensity remains finite and may even peak at the boundary. In particular, such vortices occur in M2 ocean tides around New Zealand, Madagascar, Iceland, and Svalbard, yet the conditions governing their appearance have remained elusive. Here we develop a statistical theory of vortices around islands in random two-dimensional wavefields, with and without the Coriolis effect, and test it experimentally. We determine the probabilities of vortices with different topological charges as functions of island size and Coriolis parameter. We find that island-bound vortices emerge with unexpectedly high probability, approaching 50% in non-rotating systems and nearly 100% in rotating systems. Moreover, for a broad range of parameters, the presence of a subwavelength island dramatically enhances vortex formation compared with homogeneous random wavefields. Our results explain the formation of tidal vortices around ocean islands of particular sizes (~0.1 of the characteristic wavelength) and establish a general mechanism for generating localized high-intensity vortices around defects in diverse wave systems, from water waves to nanophotonic structures.

### [94] [Data-driven identification of multiscale self-similarity and asymptotic matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16149)
*Kaixin Zhu,Nikos Bempedelis,Konstantinos Steiros*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种系统识别多尺度自相似性的数据驱动算法，无需先验物理知识。该算法在湍流槽道流和晚期均匀衰减湍流中成功识别出内外自相似性，并在中间区域恢复了相应的标度律（对数律和-5/3律），同时发现了对标度律的修正。在早期均匀衰减湍流中，算法识别出与晚期相同的内相似性但不同的外相似性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于Bempedelis等人（2025）的数据驱动框架，开发了一种系统识别多尺度自相似性的算法。该算法无需先验控制方程知识，直接从数值数据中提取多尺度自相似性。

Result: 1）在湍流槽道流和晚期均匀衰减湍流中，成功识别出内自相似性和外自相似性，并恢复了经典标度律（对数律和-5/3律）。2）在中间区域识别出独立于内外尺度的相似性表达式。3）发现了对标度律的修正：与Barenblatt（1993）提出的幂律标度相关的修正，以及对能谱近似改进的修正。4）在早期均匀衰减湍流中，识别出与晚期相同的内相似性但不同的外相似性。

Conclusion: 提出的多尺度自相似性识别算法能够从数据中系统地提取多尺度标度行为，恢复经典标度律并发现其修正，为复杂流体力学系统的数据驱动分析提供了新途径。

Abstract: A central problem in fluid mechanics is the identification of self-similarity, which reveals the underlying scaling behaviour of a flow. Recently, a data-driven framework proposed by Bempedelis et al. (2025 J. Fluid Mech., vol. 1020, A11) has enabled the extraction of single-scale self-similarity from data, without prior knowledge of the governing equations. However, many physical systems are inherently multiscale and therefore require more general approaches. Building on this foundation, we develop an algorithm for the systematic identification of multiscale self-similarity. The algorithm is first applied to two canonical fluid-mechanical problems: turbulent channel flow and late-stage homogeneous decaying turbulence characterised by classical dissipation laws. In both cases, the algorithm successfully identifies inner and outer self-similarity from numerical data and recovers the corresponding similarity expressions. In the intermediate region of both problems, the algorithm identifies similarity expressions that are independent of both the inner and outer scales, providing a novel data-driven route to recovering the corresponding scaling laws: the logarithmic law in turbulent channel flow and the -5/3 law in late-stage homogeneous decaying turbulence. Moreover, the algorithm uncovers corrections to both laws: one linked to the power-law scaling proposed by Barenblatt (1993 J. Fluid Mech., vol. 248, 513--520), and the other yielding an improved approximation of the energy spectrum. The algorithm is then applied to early-stage homogeneous decaying turbulence, characterised by the nonclassical dissipation law. It identifies the same inner similarity as in the late stage, but different outer similarity expressions.

### [95] [Design-Based Supervised Learning with Noisy Human Labels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15455)
*Robert Chew,Matthew R. Williams*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 提出PA-DSL方法，利用仲裁标签修正有噪声的人工审计标签，再使用修正后的审计信息对基于全量自动化标签的分析进行去偏。在已知审计和仲裁概率时，该方法对广泛的下游分析有效，在实验中相比仅使用仲裁标签可将RMSE降低10-17%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有矫正方法通常假设审计标签是正确无误的，但实际中人工审计标签经常包含噪声，只有部分被审计样本会经过专家或仲裁者复核。作者希望解决这种部分仲裁（adjudicated）场景下的自动化标签偏差矫正问题。

Method: 提出PA-DSL方法：首先利用仲裁标签（adjudicated cases）来矫正有噪声的人工审计标签，然后使用矫正后的审计信息对基于全量自动化标签的分析结果进行去偏。该方法要求在已知审计概率和仲裁概率的条件下使用，并通过设计基于概率抽样的框架保证估计量的有效性。

Result: 在合成数据和Wikipedia Detox半合成实验中，PA-DSL方法维持了名义覆盖水平，且相较于仅使用仲裁标签的方法，在有可恢复信号的人工噪声标签条件下，RMSE降低了10-17%。

Conclusion: PA-DSL能有效利用部分仲裁信号来矫正自动化标签的偏差，为带有噪声审计标签的实际场景提供了可行的统计推断方案，且适用于多种下游分析任务。

Abstract: Researchers increasingly use automated classifiers to label unstructured data for statistical analysis. Existing rectification methods can correct errors in these automated labels using a probability-sampled audit set, but they usually treat the audit labels as correct. In practice, human audit labels are often noisy, and only some audited items are reviewed by an expert or adjudicator. We propose Partially Adjudicated Design-Based Supervised Learning (PA-DSL), a method for this setting. It uses adjudicated cases to correct noisy human labels and then uses the corrected audit information to debias analyses based on the full set of automated labels. The estimator is valid for a broad class of downstream analyses when the audit and adjudication probabilities are known. In synthetic and Wikipedia Detox semi-synthetic experiments, PA-DSL maintains nominal coverage and reduces RMSE by 10-17% relative to using only adjudicated labels when noisy human labels contain recoverable signal.

### [96] [Retraining Seeks Stable Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15623)
*Moritz Hardt*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出"稳定信号原理"来解释重复风险最小化（重训练）在预测模型中的收敛行为：当预测目标存在模型无关的稳定信号成分时，即使模型对数据的影响很大，适当正则化的重训练也会几何级收敛到该稳定信号方向。正则化在此扮演控制表现性的角色，而非促进泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究指出当模型对数据影响较小时，重训练能达到固定点，但固定点为何自然存在、以及模型影响较大时重训练的动力学行为尚不明确。本文旨在填补这一理论空白。

Method: 从预测目标存在非零稳定信号（如物品的内在质量）的基本假设出发，利用数学证明分析正则化重训练算子的收敛性质，并将其推广到仿射重训练算子族，涵盖模型诱导特征变化、异质时变效应和非线性响应等场景。

Result: 证明了当存在非零稳定信号时，适当正则化的重复风险最小化会几何级收敛到稳定信号方向，即使模型对目标的影响相对于稳定信号任意大。正则化在此起到控制表现性（performativity）的作用，而非传统意义上的泛化正则化。

Conclusion: 稳定信号原理为理解表现性预测中的重训练动力学提供了统一视角，揭示了正则化在控制反馈循环中的新角色，并适用于语言模型中模型生成数据的稳定性解释。

Abstract: Predictive models deployed at scale influence future data, a phenomenon called performativity. And there is always one way to cope: Train the model on new data, deploy it again, and repeat. This process, called retraining or repeated risk minimization, creates a feedback loop between model and data that real-world learning systems can't avoid.
  Results on performative prediction shed light on this dynamic: If the model's influence on the data is small, retraining reaches a fixed point. What remains open is why fixed points should naturally exist, and what governs retraining when the model's influence is strong. In this work we develop a new perspective on retraining -- the stable signal principle -- that addresses these questions. We start from the assumption that the prediction target has at least some small model-independent component, a stable signal, such as the intrinsic quality of an item.
  We prove that when a nonzero stable signal exists, repeated risk minimization, suitably regularized, converges geometrically to the direction of this stable signal. This is true even if the model's influence on the target is arbitrarily large relative to the stable signal. Regularization emerges naturally as a force to control performativity, rather than to promote generalization, revealing a new facet of an old concept. We extend the analysis to a broad family of affine retraining operators under arbitrary model-induced feature changes, heterogeneous time-varying effects, and nonlinear responses. The stable signal perspective also applies to data feedback loops in language modeling, providing new explanations for the stability of language model training from model-generated data.

</details>

*Nyi Nyi Aung,Heepeom Shin,Abigail Lawlor,Adrian Stein*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于博弈论的可解释超参数-目标交互分析框架，利用Shapley效应进行全局敏感性分析，结合Pareto前沿集识别有效超参数配置并支持早期模型评估，在三种神经网络架构和多目标设定下验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有超参数优化方法缺乏对超参数与不同优化目标之间交互关系的可解释性分析，难以帮助实践者理解哪些超参数在特定目标下最为关键，从而导致优化效率低下。

Method: 采用博弈论框架，将超参数视为"玩家"，优化目标视为"游戏"；使用Shapley效应进行全局敏感性分析量化各超参数对目标的贡献度；利用Pareto前沿集识别有效超参数配置，支持早期模型评估。

Result: 在三种不同神经网络架构和多目标场景下，该框架成功揭示了各超参数对不同目标的影响力排序，有效缩小了搜索空间，并为早期模型评估提供了可解释的决策依据。

Conclusion: 该框架不是提出新的优化算法，而是提供一种可解释的分析工具，帮助实践者理解超参数与目标之间的交互关系，从而指导后续优化、缩减搜索空间并进行早期模型评估。

Abstract: This work presents a game-theoretic framework for interpretable hyperparameter-objective interaction analysis rather than proposing a new optimization algorithm. In the proposed framework, Shapley Effects are employed for global sensitivity analysis, while Pareto front sets are utilized to identify effective hyperparameter configurations and support early-stage model evaluation. The resulting analysis reveals which players (hyperparameters) are most influential with respect to different objectives in a given game (application). Consequently, the proposed framework provides interpretable insights into objective-aware hyperparameter interactions, enabling practitioners to guide subsequent optimization, reduce the search space, and perform early-stage model evaluation. The effectiveness of the proposed framework is demonstrated using three distinct neural network architectures across different problem domains under multi-objective settings.

</details>


### [98] [Deep and Probabilistic Models for Gene Regulatory Network Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16053)
*Claudia Skok Gibbs*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出两个互补框架（PMF-GRN和GLM-Prior）解决基因调控网络重建中的方法论局限和先验知识瓶颈。PMF-GRN通过概率图模型和变分推断实现原则性模型选择与不确定性量化；GLM-Prior通过微调核苷酸Transformer直接从序列预测TF-靶基因相互作用，并在酵母、小鼠、人类间泛化。两者共同构成双阶段GRN重建范式：序列先验提供可迁移初始骨架，概率推断在评价资源不完备下精炼调控估计并量化不确定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GRN重建方法存在三方面局限：1）建模假设与推断过程耦合、依赖启发式模型选择；2）评价受限于不完整参考网络和缺乏不确定性的点估计输出；3）先验知识依赖特定检测方法、难以跨物种和低表征系统转移。

Method: 1）PMF-GRN：将GRN推断构建为概率图模型，采用变分推断进行优化，实现原则性模型选择和边估计的不确定性感知。2）GLM-Prior：微调预训练的Nucleotide Transformer，直接从核苷酸序列预测TF-靶基因相互作用，并在酵母、小鼠、人类三种设置中验证泛化能力。

Result: PMF-GRN实现了不确定性感知的边估计和原则性模型选择；GLM-Prior能够跨物种（酵母、小鼠、人类）泛化预测TF-靶基因相互作用。两者结合形成双阶段GRN重建框架。

Conclusion: 序列衍生的先验知识可作为可迁移的初始骨架，概率推断则在评价资源不完备的情况下精炼调控估计并量化不确定性，两者互补解决了GRN重建中的关键瓶颈。

Abstract: Gene regulatory networks (GRNs) link transcription factor (TF) proteins to their target genes, yet reconstructing these networks from genome-wide data remains challenging under practical and methodological constraints. Many methods couple modeling assumptions to a specific inference procedure and rely on heuristic model selection, while evaluation is constrained by incomplete reference networks and point-estimate outputs that lack uncertainty. GRN reconstruction also depends on prior knowledge to constrain TF-gene interactions, yet available priors are often assay-dependent and difficult to transfer across species and less-characterized systems. In this thesis, we develop two complementary frameworks that address these limitations. In the first, PMF-GRN casts GRN inference as a probabilistic graphical model optimized by variational inference, enabling principled model selection and uncertainty-aware edge estimates. In the second, GLM-Prior addresses the prior bottleneck by fine-tuning the pretrained Nucleotide Transformer to predict TF-target gene interactions directly from nucleotide sequence, while generalizing across yeast, mouse, and human settings. Together, PMF-GRN and GLM-Prior motivate a dual-stage view of GRN reconstruction in which sequence-derived priors provide a transferable starting scaffold and probabilistic inference refines regulatory estimates with quantified uncertainty under incomplete evaluation resources.

</details>


### [99] [Cluster-Aware Matching via Laplacian Optimal Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16178)
*Gabriel Samberg,YoonHaeng Hur,Yuehaw Khoo,Nir Sharon*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 提出基于拉普拉斯最优传输（LapOT）的聚类感知匹配方法，通过二次拉普拉斯正则化项鼓励最优耦合尊重点云的聚类结构，并引入精炼同步聚类（RSC）实现跨点云的一致性分区。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在点云匹配中，点云并非无结构点集，而是具有内在聚类结构的分布样本；个体点在相干区域内可互换，因此建立鲁棒的区域间对齐比精确的点对点对应更有意义。

Method: 1) 利用点云相似图构建二次拉普拉斯项，正则化最优传输问题（LapOT）；2) 提出精炼同步聚类（RSC），利用LapOT得到的聚类感知耦合产生跨点云的一致性分区。

Result: 理论分析和实证实验均表明LapOT能产生聚类感知的匹配，实现更一致、更有意义的点云对齐。

Conclusion: LapOT有效实现了聚类感知的点云匹配，能够克服独立聚类的局限性，产生更稳定和可解释的结果。

Abstract: In many applications of matching, the point clouds to be matched are not merely unstructured sets of points but rather samples from distributions with an intrinsic cluster structure. In such cases, as individual points are often interchangeable within a coherent region, finding a robust region-to-region alignment is more desirable than establishing a precise point-to-point correspondence. To this end, we propose a novel approach for cluster-aware matching based on Laplacian Optimal Transport (LapOT). The key idea is to regularize the optimal transport problem with quadratic Laplacian terms constructed from similarity graphs of the point clouds, which encourages the optimal coupling to respect the cluster structure of both point sets. We also introduce Refined Simultaneous Clustering (RSC), a method that leverages the cluster-aware coupling obtained from LapOT to produce consistent partitions across the point sets, which can overcome the limitations of independent clustering and yield more stable and interpretable results. We demonstrate the effectiveness of our approach through theoretical analysis and empirical experiments, showing that LapOT indeed produces cluster-aware matching that leads to more consistent and meaningful alignments between point clouds.

</details>

### [100] [On the Computational Complexity of Bilevel Integer Linear Programming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15369)
*Nagisa Sugishita,Margarida Carvalho*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文证明了双层整数线性规划在一般整数变量下仍然是Σ^p_2-完全的，解决了40余年悬而未决的问题，并分析了不同结构假设对计算复杂度的影响，特别地，在上层和下层变量总数固定时证明了多项式时间可解性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决Jeroslow (1985)关于二进制变量双层整数线性规划Σ^p_2-完全性结果在一般整数变量下是否成立的开放问题，该问题已悬置40余年。

Method: 通过复杂度理论分析，将二进制变量的Σ^p_2-完全性推广到一般整数变量情形，并研究不同结构假设（如固定变量总数）对复杂度的影响。

Result: 证明了一般整数变量下双层整数线性规划仍然是Σ^p_2-完全的；同时证明在上层和下层变量总数固定时，该问题可在多项式时间内求解。

Conclusion: 双层整数线性规划在一般整数变量情形下继承了二进制变量情形的Σ^p_2-完全性，但固定变量总数可大幅降低计算复杂度至多项式时间可解。

Abstract: We investigate the computational complexity of bilevel integer linear programming. While Jeroslow~(1985) established that the decision version of this problem is $Σ^p_2$-complete when restricted to binary variables, we prove that this $Σ^p_2$-completeness persists even for general integer variables, settling a question that remained open for over 40 years. Furthermore, we analyze the impact of various structural assumptions on computational complexity. Notably, we strengthen the result of Köppe et al.~(2010) by proving polynomial-time solvability whenever the total number of upper- and lower-level variables is fixed, without any additional assumptions.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过程优化模型常包含复杂互联单元操作、动态特性和不确定性，导致大规模非线性规划问题，传统CPU求解器计算负担重。尽管新兴GPU求解器具有显著计算优势，但由于缺乏GPU兼容的过程建模工具，其在过程优化中的应用受到限制。

Method: 利用现有GPU兼容优化软件栈（ExaModels代数建模系统、MadNLP优化求解器、cuDSS线性求解器）构建GPU兼容的过程优化模型。ExaModels通过暴露重复代数结构以GPU兼容方式表述问题，MadNLP和cuDSS在GPU上求解所得非线性规划。在CO2吸收器设计问题（含进料不确定性）上验证，最小化共享塔径需满足所有场景下的平衡和水力约束。

Conclusion: 该工作流证明了GPU在过程优化中的巨大潜力，填补了GPU兼容过程建模工具的空白，为大规模过程优化问题提供高效求解方案。

Abstract: This paper presents a proof-of-concept workflow for equation-oriented process optimization that runs entirely on a GPU. Process optimization models often incorporate complex interconnected unit operations, dynamics, and uncertainties, resulting in large nonlinear programs that can be computationally demanding for conventional CPU-based solvers. Although emerging GPU-based solvers offer substantial computational benefits, their application to process optimization has been limited by the lack of GPU-compatible process modeling tools. We address this gap by prototyping the GPU-compatible process optimization models using an existing GPU-capable optimization software stack, including ExaModels (algebraic modeling system), MadNLP (optimization solver), and cuDSS (linear solver). ExaModels formulates the process optimization problem in a GPU-compatible way by exposing its repeated algebraic structure, while MadNLP and cuDSS solve the resulting nonlinear program on the GPU. This workflow is demonstrated on a CO2 absorber design problem under feed uncertainty, in which a shared column diameter is minimized subject to equilibrium and hydraulic constraints in all scenarios. For the largest case with 5,000 scenarios and 1.5 million variables, the GPU workflow achieves a speedup of approximately 21\times over a single-threaded CPU baseline using JuMP, Ipopt, and MA57.

The resulting optimality system reveals a natural Hamiltonian structure on the Wasserstein space, providing a direct link between optimal transport, Hamiltonian dynamics, and optimal control. The proposed framework extends the classical quadratic-cost theory to general Lagrangian costs and offers a unified perspective for the analysis of transport metrics generated by action functionals.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过双参数(λ₁,λ₂)参数化平均收益博弈建模双目标问题，分析可行域与帕累托前沿的凸性与分段线性结构；证明联合分母界定理（周期系数和≤2，除完全解耦情形外）；开发定向二分算法（O(n²(n+m)log M)）和牛顿追踪算法（至多|S|步2×2线性求解）。

Result: 可行域R为凸集，帕累托前沿P为具有有限个断点的凸分段线性曲线；联合分母界：任意基本环γ满足k₁(γ)+k₂(γ)≤2，除完全解耦情形外每个2×2牛顿系统满足|Δ|≤2，整数数据下所有断点为半整数坐标；定向二分算法复杂度为O(n²(n+m)log M)（伪多项式），牛顿算法至多|S|步（指数步数）；随机实例验证了定向二分算法的复杂度界，牛顿算法的最坏界通过显式对抗构造达到紧致性。

Conclusion: 双目标热带伪线性优化的帕累托前沿具有与单参数情形自然对应的凸分段线性结构；联合分母界定理是新的理论贡献；两种算法各有适用场景：定向二分法适用于有限精度需求，牛顿法适用于完整前沿刻画但最坏情况指数复杂。

Abstract: We extend the parametric mean-payoff game framework of Parsons et al. to bi-objective tropical pseudolinear optimization with general two-sided constraints. The problem is to simultaneously minimize two tropical pseudolinear objectives over the feasible set of a general two-sided system U otimes x oplus b is less than or equal to V otimes x oplus d, we characterize the Pareto front via a parametric mean-payoff game in two parameters ( lambda 1, lambda 2). The feasibility region R is convex and the Pareto front P is a convex piecewise-linear curve with finitely many breakpoints, these properties are natural extensions of the single-parameter case to two parameters. In addition, we give as a new result, the joint denominator bound: the cycle coefficients satisfy k 1( gamma ) + k 2( gamma ) is less than or equal to 2 for any elementary cycle gamma, yielding | Delta | is less than or equal to 2 for every 2 times 2 Newton system, except in the fully decoupled case, and implying that all breakpoints have half-integer coordinates for integer data. Optimality and infeasibility certificates are given in terms of the cycle structure of the parametric game. Two algorithms are developed, a directional bisection algorithm (O(n squared (n+m) log M) per direction) and a Newton scheme tracing the complete Pareto front via 2 times 2 linear solves in at most | S | steps, independent of M. The directional bisection algorithm is pseudo-polynomial in n, m and M. The Newton scheme is independent of M but requires up to |S| steps, where |S| is exponential in n. Lastly, we give numerical experiments on random instances to confirm the directional bisection complexity bound exactly; the Newton scheme's worst-case bound is not attained by random instances but is shown to be tight via explicit adversarial constructions.

### [104] [Fast and Scalable Caputo Fractional Gradient Descent via Perturbation-Preserving Memory Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15505)
*Hwanseo Lee,Junseo Lee,Hyunju Kim*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出两种降低Caputo型分数阶梯度下降（FGD）历史依赖卷积计算成本的方法（SOE递归近似和DHDC多尺度压缩），在保持记忆结构的同时将复杂度从二次降至线性，并证明在可控近似误差下仍保持单调下降和线性收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分数阶梯度下降（FGD）通过Caputo算子引入长程记忆，在病态和非凸优化中表现出更好的稳定性，但其实际应用受限于历史依赖卷积的高计算成本（随迭代次数二次增长），亟需在不破坏固有记忆结构的前提下提升计算可行性。

Method: 1) 将分数阶下降方向表达为过去梯度的离散卷积，提供统一视图；2) 提出两种互补机制降低记忆项成本：① 幂律核的指数和（SOE）近似，实现高效递归更新；② 新提出的二元层次离散卷积（DHDC），通过多尺度聚合策略压缩梯度历史。将上述近似视为理想Caputo算子的扰动进行分析。

Result: 在μ-强凸和L-光滑假设下，可控近似误差范围内，所提方法仍保持单调下降和线性收敛特性。

Conclusion: 通过SOE和DHDC两种方法，Caputo型分数阶优化可在保持其记忆结构优势的同时显著降低计算复杂度，为实际应用提供了可行的技术路径。

Abstract: Fractional gradient descent (FGD) incorporates long-range memory through Caputo-type operators and has been shown to improve stability in ill-conditioned and nonconvex optimization problems. Despite these advantages, its practical use remains limited, mainly due to the high computational cost of evaluating history-dependent convolutions, which scales quadratically with the number of iterations. In this paper, we focus on making Caputo-based optimization computationally viable without sacrificing its intrinsic memory structure. We begin by expressing the fractional descent direction as a discrete convolution over past gradients, which provides a unified view of the method. Based on this formulation, we introduce two complementary mechanisms to reduce the cost of the memory term. The first uses a sum-of-exponentials (SOE) approximation of the power-law kernel, leading to efficient recursive updates. The second approach, newly proposed in this paper as dyadic hierarchical discrete convolution (DHDC), compresses the gradient history through a multiscale aggregation strategy. Rather than treating these approximations as purely numerical accelerations, we interpret them as perturbations of the ideal Caputo operator. This viewpoint allows us to analyze how the compressed memory affects the optimization dynamics. Under standard $μ$-strong convexity and $L$-smoothness assumptions, we show that the resulting method still exhibits monotone descent and linear convergence, provided that the approximation error remains controlled.

*Thomas Perrin*

Method: 通过二次展开中的反复分部积分结合非线性余项估计，识别控制剖面的条件与迭代Lie括号的关系，证明二次障碍的存在性。

Result: 发现了控制剖面导致任意整数阶负Sobolev范数量化的二次障碍的条件，并构造了产生所有负整数阶障碍的光滑空间剖面。

Abstract: We consider the Burgers equation with a scalar control acting through a fixed spatial profile, in a regime where the linearized system is not controllable. We identify natural conditions on the control profile leading to quadratic obstructions to small-time local null-controllability, quantified by negative Sobolev norms of the control of arbitrary integer order. We show that these conditions are related to iterated Lie brackets. The proof relies on repeated integrations by parts in the quadratic expansion combined with nonlinear remainder estimates. Finally, we construct smooth spatial profiles that produce obstructions at every negative integer order.

### [106] [Polynomial-Based Solutions to Targeting Problems for Onboard Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15801)
*Adam Evans,Alberto Fossa,Roberto Armellin,Didier Henrion,Renato Zanetti*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文利用微分代数将轨迹优化问题转化为多项式优化问题（POP），并采用矩-SOS（moment-sum-of-squares）优化方法求解，在保持高精度的同时提供全局最优收敛性保证，适用于大机动、长传播时间及连续低推力场景，具备自主星上应用的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决轨道机动中的目标瞄准问题，传统非线性规划（NLP）求解器存在收敛到局部最优的风险，而线性近似方法在大机动或长传播时间条件下精度迅速退化，亟需一种兼具高精度、计算效率与可靠收敛性的方法。

Method: 首先通过微分代数计算非线性动力学和约束的高阶泰勒展开，将轨迹优化问题重新表述为多项式优化问题（POP）；然后利用矩-SOS（moment-sum-of-squares）优化求解该POP；同时提出基于二阶动力学展开的凸优化方法作为对比。针对脉冲式瞄准，将矩-SOS和凸方法与传统的NLP求解器及映射反演技术进行比较。

Result: 矩-SOS方法在精度上与传统NLP方法相当，但具有在温和假设下保证收敛到全局最优的关键优势；该方法在处理大机动和长传播时间场景时表现出色，而标准线性近似在这些条件下迅速退化；在存在较大状态误差的地月圆型限制性三体问题连续低推力保持场景中，算法性能得到验证。

Conclusion: 矩-SOS方法能够直接处理非凸约束，并将复杂的非线性动力学转化为具有可靠收敛性的形式，使其适用于自主星上应用。

Abstract: This paper solves the targeting problem focusing on accuracy, computational efficiency, and reliability. The trajectory optimization problem is first recast as a polynomial optimization problem (POP) by leveraging differential algebra to compute high-order Taylor expansions of the nonlinear dynamics and constraints. Moment-sum-of-squares (SOS) optimization is then utilized to solve this POP. A convex formulation based on a second-order expansion of the dynamics is also proposed. For impulsive targeting, the moment-SOS and convex approaches are compared against traditional nonlinear programming (NLP) solvers and map inversion techniques. Results indicate that the moment-SOS approach provides solutions as accurate as traditional NLP, but with the critical advantage of guaranteeing convergence to the global optimum under mild assumptions. Furthermore, the method excels at handling large maneuvers and long propagation times, conditions in which standard linear approximations rapidly degrade. To demonstrate its versatility, the methodology is extended to a continuous low-thrust station keeping (SK) scenario in the Earth-Moon Circular Restricted Three-Body Problem. The algorithm's performance is then evaluated in the presence of significant state errors. The ability to directly handle non-convex constraints and recast complex, nonlinear dynamics into formulations with reliable convergence properties makes the moment-SOS approach suitable for autonomous onboard applications.

</details>

### [109] [Two-Thread Coverage MCTS for SAT and XSAT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15834)
*Marcel Crasmaru*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结合WalkSAT风格rollout与双线程对称破缺初始化的MCTS求解器，在SAT和XSAT问题上取得显著效果，包括秒杀SATLIB图着色编码、解决planted 3-XOR-SAT问题、以及处理DES密钥恢复编码时达到99.9%子句满足率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SAT求解器在对称性较强的实例（如图着色、XOR-SAT）上效率不高，且缺乏有效的对称破缺初始化策略。本文旨在通过结合MCTS的探索能力与WalkSAT的局部搜索、以及双线程极性分裂初始化，提升对具有对称结构的大规模SAT/XSAT问题的求解性能。

Method: 提出一个MCTS求解器，内部使用WalkSAT风格的rollout进行节点评估；初始化阶段采用双线程对称破缺策略：一个线程从全真赋值开始，另一个从全假赋值开始，每个线程的初始Hamming距离被约束在⌊n/2⌋以内，从而在极性空间上实现覆盖。

Conclusion: 所提出的MCTS+双线程对称破缺初始化策略在多种SAT/XSAT问题上表现出色，特别是对对称性强的实例（图着色、XOR-SAT）和工业级问题（DES密钥恢复）具有显著优势；极性分裂本身可作为高效的初始化技巧，展现了方法在对称破缺和搜索平衡方面的有效性。

Abstract: We introduce a Monte-Carlo Tree Search solver for SAT and XSAT that pairs WalkSAT-style rollouts with a two-thread symmetry-breaking initialisation: one thread starts from all-true, the other from all-false, bounding each thread's initial Hamming distance to a satisfying assignment by $\lfloor n/2 \rfloor$. Empirically the solver closes 100/100 SATLIB graph-colouring encodings (flat200-479, sw100) in tens of milliseconds each, 20/20 planted 3-XOR-SAT at $n{=}200$ (median 10~s), 6/6 at $n{=}300$ (median 138~s), and one SAT Competition 2025 instance (Break-triple-04-06.xml.cnf) in 50~ms via the polarity split alone. On a full 16-round DES key-recovery encoding ($n{=}1976$, $m{=}30072$) it drives the negative-clause count from $\sim 200$ down to 24 (99.9% clauses satisfied) over 7 hours before hitting the S-box plateau.

### [110] [A Numerically-safe Branch-Price-and-Cut Algorithm for the Length-Constrained Cycle Partition Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15837)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LCCP是一个图优化问题，需要将节点集划分为尽可能少的环，且每个环的长度不能超过环中任何节点的临界时间。现有方法在求解规模和效率上存在局限，需要更有效的精确算法。

Method: 将LCCP建模为集合划分问题，采用分支定价切割（branch-price-and-cut）精确求解框架；定价子问题通过动态规划算法求解，利用问题结构实现双向搜索和对称性破缺以提升效率。

Conclusion: 所提出的精确算法在LCCP问题上取得了实质性突破，大幅提升了可求解的实例规模和求解效率。

Abstract: The length-constrained cycle partition problem (LCCP) is a graph optimization problem in which a set of nodes must be partitioned into a minimum number of cycles. Every node is associated with a critical time and the length of every cycle must not exceed the critical time of any node in the cycle. We formulate LCCP as a set partitioning model and solve it using an exact branch-price-and-cut approach. Our dynamic programming-based pricing algorithm to generate improving cycles exploits the particular structure of the pricing problem for efficient bidirectional search and symmetry breaking. Computational results show that the LP relaxation of the set partitioning model produces very strong dual bounds and our branch-price-and-cut method improves significantly over the state of the art. It is able to solve previously solved instances in a fraction of the time and closes 14 previously unsolved instances with numerically safe bounds, one of which has 76 nodes, a notable improvement over the previous limit of 52 nodes.

The signal layer employs a priority-weighted max-pressure (Priority-MP) controller to allocate green time based on occupancy-aware pressures, while the vehicle layer adapts longitudinal control based on uncertain and dynamically evolving local signal cues. A structured reward combines guidance and event-based reinforcement to align EB arrivals with green opportunities while considering energy, time, comfort, and safety. The framework uses centralized training and decentralized execution (CTDE) with parameter sharing, allowing a single DRL agent to learn from multiple buses and routes using local observations. Experiments on a real-world corridor show that PriEco-DRL reduces EB energy consumption while maintaining network efficiency and transit priority compared with fixed-time, actuated, and rule-based signal-vehicle coordination baselines. Energy- and trajectory-based analyses reveal that the improvements stem from fewer unscheduled stop-start events and smoother speed regulation under adaptive signals. The results highlight a tunable energy-time trade-off, allowing flexible operational choices through reward weighting.

### [112] [An Improved Analysis of the Last Iterate of the SubGradient Method in the Plane](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15980)

Abstract: We study the last iterate of the subGradient Method (sGM) for convex Lipschitz objectives defined on $\mathbb R^2$. This makes progress on an open problem posed by Koren and Segal in 2020 on the optimal error of the last iterate of sGM in fixed dimension.

While in the strong control limit the results reduce to known approximations from linear-quadratic control, we derive generalized amplitude equations for the co-evolution of state and costate variables describing the optimized trajectory in the weak and intermediate control regimes. These control normal forms are validated against numerical solutions of the full optimal control problem for a canonical model of a bistable biochemical switch. The bifurcation structure of the optimal control problem is analyzed in the weak control regime. Finally, we demonstrate the construction of asymptotic solutions in the long time limit in this regime using boundary-layer methods.

### [114] [Systems of nonlocal conservation laws: well-posedness and the singular limit for a nonlocal generalized Aw-Rascle-Zhang model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15408)
*Debora Amadori,Felisia Angela Chiarello,Gianmarco Cipollone,Xiaoqian Gong,Alexander Keimer*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类由交通流启发的非局部守恒律系统——非局部广义Aw-Rascle-Zhang (GARZ)模型。通过单边核函数对下游速度进行空间平均引入非局部性。利用非局部速度的不动点论证，证明了有界变差初值下弱解的存在唯一性，并建立了初值稳定性和强解在L^1中逼近弱解的性质。在额外的物理假设下，得到了密度的最大值原理或不变区域估计。研究了非局部核趋近Dirac分布的奇异极限，在附加假设下证明了收敛到唯一局部熵解。提供了数值模拟并讨论了开放问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交通流中的经典GARZ模型是局部模型，但实际交通中驾驶员的感知和反应涉及非局部信息（如前车速度的空间平均）。为更真实地刻画交通流动力学，需引入非局部项并严格分析其数学性质。

Method: 采用不动点论证处理非局部速度耦合；利用有界变差空间和L^1框架进行弱解存在唯一性分析；通过奇异极限分析（核→Dirac）建立与局部熵解的联系。

Result: 证明了非局部GARZ模型弱解的存在唯一性和稳定性；得到了密度最大值原理和不变区域估计；在奇异极限下证明了收敛到唯一局部熵解。

Conclusion: 非局部GARZ模型在数学上是适定的，且在非局部核趋于Dirac时恢复为局部熵解，验证了非局部模型作为局部模型推广的合理性。

Abstract: In this paper, we study a system of nonlocal conservation laws motivated by traffic flow: a nonlocal version of the generalized Aw-Rascle-Zhang (GARZ) model. The nonlocality arises from downstream spatial averaging of the velocity by a one-sided kernel. We prove the existence and uniqueness of weak solutions for initial data of bounded variation via a fixed-point argument in the nonlocal velocity. We also establish stability with respect to the initial datum and an approximation of weak solutions by strong solutions in $L^1$. Under additional, physically meaningful assumptions on the velocity and the initial datum, we obtain either a maximum principle for the density or invariant-region estimates. Finally, we study the singular limit as the nonlocal kernel converges to a Dirac distribution. Indeed, under additional assumptions, convergence to the unique local entropy solution can be proved. Some numerical simulations are provided, and the paper concludes with a discussion of open problems.

### [115] [On the Schrödinger--Bopp--Podolsky system with indefinite potential: ground states, multiplicity and exponential decay](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15584)
*Ting Xiao,Fan Wang,Li-Feng Yin*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有不定势的薛定谔-博普-波多尔斯基系统，通过局部链接论证、莫尔斯理论、极小化技术和对称山路定理，证明了非平凡解的存在性、指数衰减性、基态解以及无穷多解的存在性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有不定势（薛定谔算子-Δ+V具有有限维负空间）的薛定谔-博普-波多尔斯基系统，该类系统在物理中具有重要应用，但不定势情形下的解的存在性尚未得到充分研究。

Method: 采用局部链接论证和莫尔斯理论证明非平凡解的存在性；利用极小化技术获得基态解；在非线性项为奇函数时，运用对称山路定理得到无界解序列。

Result: 证明了非平凡解的存在性，并证明这些解在无穷远处呈指数衰减；通过极小化方法得到了基态解；当f(x,u)关于u为奇函数时，得到了一个无界解序列。

Conclusion: 在不定位势和适当非线性条件下，薛定谔-博普-波多尔斯基系统存在非平凡解、基态解及无穷多解，且解具有指数衰减性。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the Schrödinger--Bopp--Podolsky system
  \begin{equation*}
  \begin{cases}
  -Δu + V(x)u + φu = f(x,u), & \text{in } \mathbb{R}^3,
  -Δφ+ a^2 Δ^2 φ= 4πu^2, & \text{in } \mathbb{R}^3.
  \end{cases}
  \end{equation*}
  We consider the case where the potential \(V\) is indefinite so that the Schrödinger operator \(-Δ+ V\) has a finite-dimensional negative space. Under suitable assumptions on the potential \(V\) and nonlinearity $f(x,u)$, we prove the existence of nontrivial solutions via a local linking argument and Morse theory. Moreover, these solutions are shown to decay exponentially at infinity. Additionally, a ground state solution is obtained by minimization techniques. Finally, if \(f(x,u)\) is odd with respect to \(u\), we obtain an unbounded sequence of solutions using the symmetric mountain pass theorem.

</details>


### [116] [Riesz transform and its related inequalities for degenerate elliptic operators of Grushin type](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15599)
*Dangyang He*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了Grushin型退化椭圆算子的Riesz变换的$L^p$有界性及逆Riesz不等式。当退化变量维数至少为2时，证明了Riesz变换的全范围$L^p$有界性；在一维弱退化情形得到了精确范围（含端点障碍）；在一维强退化情形恢复了全范围有界性，揭示了奇异集行为的显著转变。主要方法包括：面向Friedrichs延拓的显式Poisson核与Green核构造，以及隔离Riesz核临界部分的调和消去法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解退化椭圆算子（Grushin型）的Riesz变换在$L^p$空间中的有界性机制，特别是奇异集维数对正则性的影响，以及退化程度（弱/强）导致的截然不同的有界性行为。

Method: 建立了Grushin调和函数在奇异集附近的逆Hölder理论；利用Friedrichs延拓构造显式Poisson核与Green核；提出调和消去法（harmonic annihilation method）将Riesz核的临界部分隔离分析。

Result: 退化变量维数≥2时Riesz变换全范围$L^p$有界；一维弱退化情形获得精确有界范围（含$p=1$端点障碍）；一维强退化情形恢复全范围有界性；同时得到了同类算子的本质上精确的逆Riesz不等式。

Conclusion: 揭示了Grushin型算子中退化维数与退化强度对有界性范围的精确影响，奇异集从低维（1维）到高维（≥2维）以及从弱退化到强退化的转变是决定性的。所发展的方法为更一般退化椭圆算子的分析提供了新工具。

Abstract: We study the $L^p$ boundedness of the Riesz transform and the reverse Riesz inequality for degenerate elliptic operators of Grushin type. We prove full-range $L^p$ boundedness of the Riesz transform when the degenerate variable has dimension at least two, and obtain the sharp range in the one-dimensional weakly degenerate case, including the endpoint obstruction. In the strongly degenerate one-dimensional regime, we recover full-range boundedness, revealing a striking transition in the behavior of the singular set.
  The proof develops a reverse Hölder theory for Grushin harmonic functions near the singular set. The main ingredients are explicit Poisson and Green kernel constructions adapted to the Friedrichs extension and a harmonic annihilation method which isolates the critical part of the Riesz kernel. These techniques illuminate the mechanism behind both the boundedness and unboundedness phenomena, and yield essentially sharp reverse Riesz inequalities for the same class of operators.

### [117] [The structure of the solution to the generalized Stokes equations and a new method for solving them](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15685)
*Arian Novruzi*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文揭示了广义Stokes方程解的一种特殊结构：速度场可分解为两个散度自由的Helmholtz型矢量场之和，压力场可分解为外力的Helmholtz分解势与一个称为"固体压力"的调和函数之和。固体压力通过求解一个自伴 coercive 边界方程来修正速度场的法向边界条件。该方法在数值上解耦了速度与压力，仅需求解边界耦合的Helmholtz型方程和一个边界方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找广义Stokes方程解的内在结构，通过理论分解将速度场与压力场解耦，以简化数值求解过程，避免直接处理不可压缩约束。

Method: 将速度u分解为两个散度自由、满足矢量Helmholtz型方程的场ω和θ之和；将压力p分解为外力的Helmholtz分解势π与固体压力q之和。固体压力q通过求解一个自伴coercive算子的线性边界方程来确定，以修正ω+θ的法向Dirichlet边界条件。

Result: 证明了无论固体压力q如何选取，ω+θ均满足除法向Dirichlet边界条件外的广义Stokes方程；固体压力q的作用是强制ω+θ满足完整的Dirichlet边界条件。方法在数值上解耦速度与压力，仅需求解Helmholtz型矢量方程（边界耦合）和一个边界方程。

Conclusion: 该方法从数值角度具有吸引力：无需直接求解不可压缩约束，解耦了速度与压力，仅需处理Helmholtz型方程和边界方程。数值实验验证了该方法的有效性。

Abstract: We show that the solution to the generalized Stokes equations with Dirichlet boundary conditions in dimension two or three has a particular structure. Namely, the velocity $u$ is the superposition of two velocity fields $ω$ and $θ$, $u=ω+θ$, each of them being divergence-free and solving vector Helmholtz-like equations. The right hand sides of these equations involve the rotational component of the Helmholtz decomposition of the external force, and a harmonic function $q$, called solid pressure. Similarly, the fluid pressure $p$ is the superposition of the potential $π$ of Helmholtz decomposition of the external force, and of the solid pressure $q$, $p=π+q$. It turns out that regardless the solid pressure $q$, $ω+θ$ satisfies the generalized Stokes equations, except the normal component of the Dirichlet boundary condition. The role of the solid pressure, which solves a linear boundary equation with a self-adjoint coercive operator, is to constrain $ω+θ$ to satisfy even the normal component of the Dirichlet boundary condition.
  The method is attractive from the numerical viewpoint. It decouples the velocity from the pressure and does not solve the incompressibility constraint directly. It requires only the solution of Helmholtz-like vector equations coupled on the boundary, and of a boundary equation. In the last section we present two methods for solving numerically the generalized Stokes equations, and some results to demonstrate the efficiency of our approach.

</details>

As an application, we prove a new estimate in the quantitative immersability of thin prestrained films, setting the scaling exponent of the infimum of non-Euclidean energies in presence of an arbitrary prestrain metric, and in the limit of the film's vanishing thickness, at $\frac{4α_0}{α_0+1}$.

### [121] [Asymptotic expansions of the eigenvalues and norms for perturbations about the Falkner--Skan solution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15858)
*Carlos Lozano,Jorge Ponsin*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文推导了Chen-Libby扰动问题关于Falkner-Skan边界层剖面的大模渐近展开式，发现当压力梯度参数β非零时，壁面层会以相对阶Λ^{-1/3}奇异扰动内层Bessel问题，产生新的s^{-1/3}壁面诱导贡献项（领先于Brown的s^{-1/2}修正项），该新项在Blasius极限下消失，恢复Brown的序关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用匹配渐近展开方法，分析大模参数Λ下Falkner-Skan边界层剖面的三层结构（外层、中层和壁面层），并引入新的壁面层修正项处理β≠0时对Bessel问题的奇异扰动。

Result: 发现Falkner-Skan壁面展开在相对阶Λ^{-1/3}处奇异扰动内层Bessel问题，产生新的s^{-1/3}壁面诱导贡献项（s=n-1，n为大特征值指标），该新项领先于Brown的s^{-1/2}修正项；在Blasius极限下新项消失，恢复Brown序关系。同时给出了Chen-Libby范数的渐近估计。

Conclusion: 通过与β=1/2的直接数值打靶计算结果对比，验证了特征值和特征函数范数渐近公式的收敛性，证实了新壁面修正项的作用。

Abstract: We derive large-mode asymptotic expansions for the eigenvalues and eigenfunction norms of the Chen-Libby perturbation problem about Falkner-Skan boundary-layer profiles. The analysis extends Brown's matched-asymptotic construction for the Blasius problem to Falkner-Skan solutions with positive wall shear -- both favorable gradients and the upper branch of the mild adverse range. Although the outer and middle layers retain the same structure as in the Blasius case, the wall layer changes qualitatively when the pressure-gradient parameter $β$ is nonzero: the Falkner-Skan wall expansion singularly perturbs the inner Bessel problem at relative order $Λ^{-1/3}$, where $Λ$ is the large eigenvalue parameter. This produces a new wall-induced contribution $s^{-1/3}$ (where $s=n-1$ and $n$ is the large eigenvalue index) to the large-mode eigenvalue expansion, ahead of Brown's $s^{-1/2}$ correction. The new term vanishes in the Blasius limit, where Brown's ordering is recovered. The matched eigenfunction also yields asymptotic estimates for the Chen-Libby norms. The eigenvalue and norm formulae are compared with direct numerical shooting calculations for $β=1/2$, showing the expected asymptotic convergence and confirming the role of the new wall correction.

### [122] [Modified compensating functions for the incompressible Euler--Vlasov--Fokker--Planck system: Global classical solutions and pointwise-in-space decay](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15878)
*Jinkai Ni*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了三维全空间不可压缩Euler-Vlasov-Fokker-Planck系统在Maxwell平衡态附近的Cauchy问题。通过构造含有限秩斜对称修正的四矩补偿器，结合不可压缩约束与耗散结构的退化分析，证明了小初始条件下唯一全局经典解的存在性，并建立了正阶导数的(1+t)^{-1/2}衰减率，无需低阶积分假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Euler-VFP系统的Fokker-Planck算子和粒子-流体阻力耗散相对动量，但无法单独控制共同的粒子-流体动量（傅里叶变量中表现为横向动量分量的退化），导致经典四矩补偿器缺乏强制性。为克服这一退化性并建立全局适定性与衰减估计，需要新的补偿机制。

Method: 在经典四矩补偿器中加入由二阶Hermite模式构造的有限秩斜对称修正；利用动能项与流体阻力项之间的抵消关系以及不可压缩约束；构建补偿傅里叶能量；仅使用动理学扰动的空间导数进行高阶能量论证，无需混合(x,v)导数估计；构造正阶Lyapunov泛函。

Result: 对充分小的初始数据(u0,f0)∈H^N×L_v^2(H^N)，N≥4，得到唯一全局经典解；正阶空间导数在L^2范数下和相应的逐点空间范数下均具有(1+t)^{-1/2}衰减率；直接耗散变量u−J(f)和{I−P0}f在L^2范数下以相同速率衰减；无需对初始数据施加L^1可积性或低频假设。

Conclusion: 首次建立了不可压缩Euler-VFP系统的正阶和零阶衰减估计，弥补了该系统中由于动量耗散退化导致的补偿理论空白。

Abstract: We consider the Cauchy problem for the incompressible Euler-Vlasov-Fokker-Planck (Euler-VFP) system in the whole space \(\mathbb R^3\) near the global Maxwellian equilibrium. The Fokker-Planck operator and the particle-fluid drag dissipate the relative momentum but do not separately control the common particle-fluid momentum; in Fourier variables, this degeneracy occurs in the transverse momentum components. To recover the missing coercivity, we augment the classical four-moment compensator with a finite-rank skew-adjoint correction constructed from second-order Hermite modes. Combined with the cancellation between the kinetic and fluid drag terms and the incompressibility constraint, the resulting compensated Fourier energy yields a unique global classical solution for sufficiently small initial data $(u_0,f_0)\in H^N\times L_v^2(H^N)$, with $N\geq 4$. The high-order energy argument involves only spatial derivatives of the kinetic perturbation and requires no mixed \(x\)-\(v\) derivative estimates. We further construct a positive-order Lyapunov functional and establish the decay rate \((1+t)^{-1/2}\) for all positive-order spatial derivatives in the \(L^2\)-norm and for the corresponding pointwise-in-space norms, without any additional \(L^1\) integrability or low-frequency assumption on the initial data. Although no uniform algebraic decay rate is asserted for the zero-order energy of \((u,f)\), the directly dissipative variables \(u-J(f)\) and \(\{\mathbf I-\mathbf P_0\}f\) decay in the \(L^2\)-norm at the same rate, where $ J(f)=\int_{\mathbb R^3}v\sqrt M f\,{\rm d}v$ denotes the particle momentum and \(\mathbf P_0\) is the orthogonal projection onto \(\operatorname{span}\{\sqrt M,v_1\sqrt M,v_2\sqrt M,v_3\sqrt M\}\). To the best of our knowledge, these positive-order and zero-order decay estimates have not previously been established for the incompressible Euler-VFP system.

Abstract: We study the joint diffusive-mean field limit for a system of weakly interacting kinetic Langevin dynamics, extending the results of Delgadino, Gvalani and Pavliotis (Arch. Ration. Mech. Anal., 2021) to the hypoelliptic/hypocoercive case. We show that, in the absence of phase transitions, the two limits commute, and we calculate the covariance matrix of the limiting Brownian motion using the Green-Kubo/Kipnis-Varadhan formula. However, at low temperatures, and in the presence of phase transitions, the two limits may not commute. We demonstrate our findings by providing a detailed analysis of the diffusive-mean field limit for the $O(2)$ model in a magnetic field. Our analysis is based on the systematic use of recently developed hypocoercivity techniques, together with an appropriate linearization of the mean field McKean-Vlasov-Fokker-Planck partial differential equation.

### [124] [Positive and nodal solutions for the Minkowski mean curvature equation: multiplicity and asymptotics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15956)

TL;DR: 本文研究了Minkowski空间中平均曲率算子的Dirichlet问题，分析了参数λ和μ对解多重性的联合影响。当λ不属于Dirichlet-Laplace谱且μ足够大时，存在全局极小解（负作用能级）和min-max解（正作用能级）。全局极小解在μ→∞时趋近于dist(·,∂Ω)，饱和几何约束|∇u|≤1；min-max解则一致塌缩到零。在球域中，利用打靶法证明了对于任意λ≥0且μ足够大时，存在任意多个节点径向解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Minkowski空间中平均曲率算子的Dirichlet问题中参数λ和μ对解多重性的联合影响，尤其是当非线性项h在u=0处超线性时，参数如何协同作用产生多个解。

Method: 采用Szulkin的非光滑泛函方法，结合全局极小化与min-max方法。对于球域情形，使用打靶法（shooting approach）构造节点径向解。

Result: 当λ不属于Dirichlet-Laplace谱且μ足够大时，存在全局极小解（负作用能级）和min-max解（正作用能级）。全局极小解在μ→∞时收敛到dist(·,∂Ω)，饱和几何约束；min-max解则一致收敛到零。给出了λ和μ的某些取值下的不存在性判据。球域中，对于任意λ≥0且μ足够大，存在任意多个节点径向解。

Conclusion: 参数λ和μ的联合作用可诱导Minkowski空间中平均曲率方程的多解性，且解的极限行为依赖于解的类型（全局极小解饱和约束，min-max解塌缩），球域中可构造任意多节点径向解。

Abstract: We consider the Dirichlet problem for the mean curvature operator in Minkowski space, \[ -\operatorname{div}\left(\frac{\nabla u}{\sqrt{1-|\nabla u|^2}}\right) = λu + μh(x,u) \quad \text{in } Ω, \qquad u = 0 \quad \text{on } \partialΩ, \] in a bounded domain $Ω\subset \mathbb{R}^N$, where $λ, μ$ are real parameters, and the nonlinearity $h$ is superlinear at $u = 0$. In particular, we study the combined effect of the parameters $λ,\,μ$ on the multiplicity of solutions. In the general setting, following Szulkin's approach for nonsmooth functionals, we prove the existence, for $λ$ not belonging to the spectrum of the Dirichlet Laplacian and $μ$ sufficiently large, of a global minimizing solution (with negative action level) and of a min-max solution (with positive action level). Moreover, we characterize the limiting profiles of these solutions as $μ\to +\infty$. More precisely, when the global minimizer is positive, its limit profile is $\mathrm{dist}(\cdot,\partialΩ)$, thus saturating, in the limit, the geometric constraint $|\nabla u|\le1$, while min-max solutions collapse uniformly to zero as $μ\to+\infty$. A nonexistence criterion is also given for suitable values of $λ$ and $μ$. Finally, when the domain $Ω$ is a ball, using a shooting approach, we establish the existence of arbitrarily many nodal radial solutions for every $λ\ge 0$ and for $μ$ sufficiently large.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入ε-δ两参数族模型，利用Green-Kubo公式表征增强扩散系数，通过减去确定性宏观修正后重标度涨落收敛到线性化Navier-Stokes方程驱动的乘性时空白噪声高斯场。

Result: 在d=2,3维次临界区域ε=o(δ)下证明了大数定律；在二维ε=o(δ^{1+ι})下识别了涨落的中心极限定理。

Abstract: We study randomly advected incompressible Navier-Stokes equations, where the advecting field is a mean-zero, divergence-free, space-time stationary velocity field with smooth order-one correlations. We introduce a two-parameter family of models in which the advection is accelerated on a fast temporal scale $\varepsilon^2$ and has spatial correlation length $δ$; the critical regime $\varepsilon = δ$ corresponds to the natural parabolic scaling of the Navier-Stokes equation. In the full subcritical regime $\varepsilon = o (δ)$, we prove a law of large numbers in dimensions $d = 2, 3$: the solutions converge to a deterministic Navier--Stokes system with an enhanced diffusion coefficient given by a Green-Kubo formula. In two space dimensions, under the slightly stronger assumption $\varepsilon = o (δ^{1 + ι})$ for some $ι> 0$, we identify the leading-order fluctuations: after subtracting deterministic macroscopic corrections satisfying a nonlinear system of Navier-Stokes type, the rescaled fluctuations converge to a Gaussian field solving a linearized Navier-Stokes equation driven by multiplicative space-time white noise.

### [129] [Fragmented ETH: Prethermalization, Timescales, and Ensemble Inequivalence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15350)
*C. L. Sriram,Soumya Kanti Pal,Lea F. Santos*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究具有强长程相互作用的有限量子系统如何趋近热平衡。近乎守恒量导致希尔伯特空间碎片化，能谱分裂为多个能带，从而产生异常缓慢的两阶段热化过程（含预热平台）。作者揭示了哪些观测量和初态会表现出或规避预热平台的机制，发展了微扰理论给出平台高度与时间尺度的解析表达式。提出碎片化本征态热化假说（fETH），其有限尺寸标度遵循对称性选择定则。该能带分辨描述导致微正则系综与正则系综的不等价性，无需平衡相变即可解释系综不等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解强长程相互作用有限量子系统在希尔伯特空间碎片化条件下的热化机制，解释预热平台的产生条件与非普适性，建立碎片化系统中的热化理论框架。

Method: 解析分析近乎守恒量导致的能谱能带结构；发展微扰理论推导预热平台高度与时间尺度；提出碎片化本征态热化假说（fETH）；分析有限尺寸标度中的对称性选择定则。

Result: 发现两阶段热化过程非普适，识别了决定预热平台是否出现的机制；给出了平台高度和时间尺度的解析表达式；建立了fETH框架，揭示了有限尺寸标度的对称性选择定则；解释了微正则系综与正则系综的不等价性。

Conclusion: 希尔伯特空间碎片化系统可通过能带分辨的fETH描述热化行为，系综不等价性源于能带结构而非平衡相变，该理论适用于广泛的具有碎片化特征的哈密顿量。

Abstract: We investigate how finite quantum systems with strong long-range interactions approach thermal equilibrium. Nearly conserved quantities inherited from the fully connected limit fragment the Hilbert space and give rise to a many-body spectrum split into energy bands. As a result, equilibration becomes anomalously slow and proceeds through long-lived prethermal plateaus. This two-stage equilibration process is, however, not universal. We uncover the mechanism that determines which observables and initial states exhibit, or evade, prethermal plateaus. We also develop a perturbative theory that provides analytical expressions for both the height of the prethermal plateau and its timescale. Despite the lack of global ergodicity, quantum chaos develops within individual energy bands, enabling the definition of microcanonical ensembles within the bands. This supports a band-resolved formulation of thermalization, which we term fragmented eigenstate thermalization hypothesis (fETH). Unlike conventional ETH, finite-size scaling in fETH obeys a symmetry-imposed selection rule that restricts which system sizes can be compared. This band-resolved description has direct consequences for equilibrium statistical mechanics. While microcanonical ensembles remain confined to a single band, canonical ensembles mix different bands. This mismatch explains ensemble inequivalence without invoking equilibrium phase transitions. Our results apply to a broad class of Hamiltonians exhibiting Hilbert-space fragmentation.

### [130] [Scaling regimes of the Kuramoto-Sivashinsky equation from the functional renormalization group](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15784)
*Liubov Gosteva,Nicolás Wschebor,Léonie Canet*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用光滑截止的泛函重整化群(FRG)框架建立KS模型的流方程，研究其在大尺度下的行为。

Result: KS方程的FRG流在大尺度下流向KPZ不动点；二点关联函数展现出三个普适标度区：KPZ区(z=3/2)、EW区(z=2)和inviscid区(z=1)；inviscid区源于有效粘度的消失。

Abstract: We revisit the renormalization group (RG) approach to the one-dimensional stochastic Kuramoto-Sivashinsky (KS) equation and show that previous approaches based on perturbative Wilsonian RG with a sharp cutoff are not valid, even though they yield a qualitatively correct picture. The reason is that taking momentum derivatives while using the sharp cutoff is not well-defined in some cases and leads to intrinsic divergencies. This is a well-known problem of Wilsonian RG, which can be simply cured by using a smooth cutoff, and employing the functional renormalization group (FRG) framework. We establish the flow equations for the KS model within the FRG, and demonstrate that it flows to the Kardar-Parisi-Zhang (KPZ) fixed point at large scales. We then calculate the full two-point correlation function over a wide range of momenta and frequencies. We show that it exhibits three universal scaling regimes that we characterize: the KPZ regime (with dynamical exponent $z=3/2$), the Edwards-Wilkinson regime (with $z=2$) and the recently discovered inviscid regime (with $z=1$). The latter develops over an extended range of large wavenumbers and originates from the vanishing of the effective viscosity. Lastly, we investigate the large-scale behavior of the deterministic KS equation by studying the limit of vanishing noise and we determine the scales where the KPZ regime can emerge in the deterministic case.

### [131] [Ultrametric organization of energy landscapes on random Erdős--Rényi graphs: topological origin of barrier hierarchy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15902)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在Erdős–Rényi图上给每个顶点赋随机自由能（均匀分布，宽度ΔF），用Kramers跃迁率建模动力学。通过速率矩阵的谱分解构建吸引盆之间的动力学马氏度量，进行V=5000顶点、E=5000边的计算实验，并证明极限定理。

Abstract: We investigate the ultrametric organization of energy landscapes defined on sparse random Erdős--Rényi graphs. Each graph vertex is assigned a random free energy from a uniform distribution over an interval of width $ΔF$, and the kinetics are modeled by a Markov process with Kramers transition rates. Using spectral decomposition of the rate matrix, we construct a kinetic Mahalanobis metric between basins of attraction. Computational experiments for graphs with $V=5000$ vertices and $E=5000$ edges show that the degree of nontrivial ultrametricity increases monotonically from $\approx42\%$ for $ΔF=10$ kJ/mol to $\approx96\%$ for $ΔF=1000$ kJ/mol. We prove a limit theorem: as $ΔF\to\infty$, the logarithmic asymptotics of this metric converge pointwise to the classical single-linkage ultrametric. For finite $ΔF$, corrections from suboptimal paths are exponentially suppressed with increasing $ΔF$, so that the metric becomes asymptotically ultrametric. Our results suggest that ultrametricity is a universal property of sparse, locally tree-like networks with rugged energy landscapes in the limit of large energy spreads.

### [132] [Zigzag ordering, defects, and anomalous relaxation in antiferromagnetic Kuramoto lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15911)

Conclusion: 确定性和非线性动力学与几何阻挫结合可产生异常缓慢粗化和新的普适类，为理解阻挫系统中弛豫行为提供新视角。

The local persistence probability follows a stretched-exponential form, $(P(t)\sim \exp(-c t^α))$, with $(α=1/4)$. These exponents are observed are independent of the magnitude of the coupling, which merely rescales the characteristic time scale. The equality $(α=δ=1/4)$ together with (z=2) is consistent with a distinct universality class. These results demonstrate that deterministic nonlinear dynamics and geometric frustration alone are sufficient to generate slow relaxation and anomalous scaling, without quenched disorder or stochastic noise. A continuum approximation and the corresponding coarse-grained partial differential equation provide a theoretical explanation for the observed anomalous exponents, while linear stability analysis accounts for the emergence of the zigzag ordered state. In two dimensions, geometric frustration inhibits complete ordering and gives rise to long-lived metastable domain-wall structures. An initial transient defect decay is observed before crossover and saturation. These results demonstrate how frustration and continuous phase variables can fundamentally modify coarsening dynamics and generate anomalously slow relaxation in deterministic many-body systems.

### [133] [Nonequilibrium thermodynamics of feedback-control: a phase-space perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16186)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 推导了通用反馈控制系统的涨落关系，引入广义的"不可用信息"概念，并通过有限分辨率Szilard引擎进行数值验证。

Result: 在高分辨率极限下，妖获取的信息量发散，但可提取功保持有限，原因在于同等量级的信息变得不可用（无法用于提取有用功）。

Abstract: Maxwell demons can convert knowledge into thermodynamic advantage by using measurement-acquired information. Here, I address this problem by deriving fluctuation relations for general feedback-controlled systems, including such singular cases. The central quantity is a generalized notion of unavailable information: a portion of the acquired information that cannot be used to extract useful work. Finally, a Szilard engine with finite resolution illustrates these results. In the high-resolution limit, the information acquired by the demon may diverge, yet the extractable work remains finite. This work shows that this occurs because an equally divergent amount of information becomes unavailable.

### [134] [Contour Degree of Amoebas of Complete Intersections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15424)
*Mounir Nisse*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Lang--Shapiro--Shustin关于超曲面实形轮廓实度的普适上界理论推广到任意余维数的光滑完全交线情形，填补高余维情形下实形轮廓实度估计的空白。

Method: 1) 引入对数共轭法框架：对数共轭丛、对数Grassmann映射、行列式秩条件；2) 在对数共轭局部坐标下，通过Schur补方程定义临界轨迹；3) 分n≥2r和n<2r两种情形推导显式普适轮廓实度估计；4) 用Bernstein定理替换总次数论证，得到由Newton多面体决定的稀疏混合体积界。

Result: 得到了光滑完全交线实形轮廓实度的普适上界（分n≥2r和n<2r两种情形），以及更尖锐的稀疏混合体积界，建立了高余维情形下Lang--Shapiro--Shustin理论的类比。

Conclusion: 对数共轭法几何为实形轮廓提供了新的几何解释，且稀疏混合体积界通常比普适界更优。

Abstract: We establish the first universal upper bounds for the real degree of the contour of the amoeba of a smooth complete intersection in the algebraic torus. Our approach extends the Pfaffian method of Lang--Shapiro--Shustin from hypersurfaces to arbitrary codimension by introducing a logarithmic conormal framework based on the logarithmic conormal bundle, the logarithmic Grassmann map, and determinantal rank conditions. We prove that, on suitable logarithmic conormal charts, the critical locus is locally defined by Schur--complement equations arising from the logarithmic conormal matrix. This yields explicit universal contour-degree estimates in both regimes $n\ge 2r$ and $n<2r$. We further replace total-degree arguments by Bernstein's theorem to obtain sparse mixed-volume bounds determined by the Newton polytopes of the transformed equations. These estimates are frequently much sharper than the corresponding universal bounds and provide a higher-codimensional analogue of the Lang--Shapiro--Shustin theory together with a new geometric interpretation of amoeba contours through logarithmic conormal geometry.

</details>

Abstract: We derive new upper bounds for the real degree of the contour of the amoeba of algebraic curves and hypersurfaces. Our approach refines the Pfaffian method of Lang--Shapiro--Shustin by replacing large total-degree estimates with logarithmic-conormal elimination and sparse mixed-volume techniques based on the transformed Newton polytopes. ### [136] [Order and Pascal depth of Pascal finite automorphisms of the plane](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15466)
*Elżbieta Adamus,Zbigniew Hajto*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究特征为p>0的域K上仿射平面的Pascal有限自同构，证明其阶由Pascal深度决定，且阶谱限于{1,p,p^2}，深度有界于p²。通过Jung-van der Kulk融合积和Serre树定理给出多项式群GA₂(K)的纯群论证明。构造实例表明p²阶和p²深度均可达到，并指出高维情形无界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究正特征域上仿射平面自同构的Pascal有限性质与阶之间的关系，特别是确定阶的可能取值和Pascal深度的上界。

Method: 结合Dolgachev关于平面Cremona群的定理，利用Jung-van der Kulk融合积和Serre树定理给出纯群论证明，并通过Witt向量和显式 tame 自同构G_p构造达到边界的例子。

Result: Pascal有限平面自同构的阶谱为{1,p,p²}，Pascal深度上界为p²；给出了多项式群GA₂(K)的独立证明；构造了达到阶p²（长度2的Witt向量）和深度p²（显式自同构G_p）的实例；高维情形下阶和深度均无界。

Conclusion: 揭示了正特征域上仿射平面自同构在Pascal有限性条件下阶与深度的精确刻画，与高维情形形成对比。

Abstract: Let $K$ be a field of characteristic $p>0$. For a Pascal finite automorphism $F$ of the affine plane we show that its order is determined by its Pascal depth, $|F|=p^{\lceil\log_pτ_K(F)\rceil}$, and that, combined with Dolgachev's theorem on the plane Cremona group, this pins the order spectrum of Pascal finite plane automorphisms to $\{1,p,p^2\}$ and bounds the Pascal depth by $τ_K(F)\le p^2$. For the polynomial group $\text{GA}_2(K)$ we give a second, independent proof of the order-$p^2$ ceiling, a purely group-theoretic argument from the Jung--van der Kulk amalgam and Serre's tree theorem, using no birational geometry. We prove that the bound is sharp in two independent senses. Order~$p^2$ is attained by the length-two Witt vectors, and Pascal depth $p^2$ is attained by an explicit tame automorphism $G_p$, for which we give a characteristic-free proof that $τ_K(G_p)=p^2$. We contrast the plane with higher dimensions, where both order and depth are unbounded.

### [137] [Tropicalizing polynomial strata](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15473)
*Yan Mary He,Chenxi Wu*

Main category: math.AG

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Let ${\rm Poly}_D(\vecμ^*)$ be the ramification stratum in the parameter space of degree $D \geq 2$ complex polynomials consisting of polynomials with ramification profile $\vecμ^*$. In this paper, we introduce a space $\mathcal{T}_D(\vecμ^*)$ of framed decorated polynomial trees and identify it with the dynamical tropicalization of ${\rm Poly}_D(\vecμ^*)$.
  A non-trivial point is that the tropicalization of ${\rm Poly}_D(\vecμ^*)$ is not available a priori, as the stratum does not come with a previously known proper toroidal compactification. We resolve this issue by identifying ${\rm Poly}_D(\vecμ^*)$ with a rigidified framed Hurwitz space. Using the twisted admissible cover compactification, together with additional rigidifying data, we construct a proper toroidal compactification and hence an associated Berkovich skeleton.   In this paper we explore the more general setting of a curve defined over a field of any characteristic, and $H$ a group admitting a cyclic subgroup of index two. Then we provide some classification results about (non-dihedral) groups of size larger than $4g(\mathcal{X})+4$ admitting a cyclic subgroup of index $2$.

The Galois action on their Picard groups factors through the Weyl group $W(D_n)$, reducing rationality to a condition on signed permutation types. ### [142] [Degenerations of multisingularities and Artin algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16022)
*Jakub Koncki,Richárd Rimányi*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究交换、结合、有限维复Artin代数的退化层次结构，提出基于奇点理论的稳定层次，并证明该层次可通过自同构群和Thom多项式确定，同时扩展了经典代数变形理论的退化框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的退化研究依赖于Hilbert方案，而本文希望通过奇点理论（稳定映射芽与局部代数的对应关系）引入新的退化概念，从而建立更自然的偏序结构，并克服经典变形理论中要求代数维数固定的限制。

Method: 引入奇点理论中的稳定层次（stable hierarchy）概念，基于稳定映射芽的奇点与局部代数之间的对应关系；利用Kazarian建立的等变示性类理论（多奇点的Thom多项式）作为关键工具，通过代入合适的Thom多项式来刻画退化层次；将代数自同构群作为对称数据来判定较大维度范围内的退化关系。

Result: 主要结果一：在广泛维度范围内，稳定层次可纯粹由对称数据（代数或奇点的自同构群）决定，计算退化的偏序集成为算法性问题。主要结果二：奇点理论定义的稳定层次是经典代数变形理论退化层次的扩展——变形理论要求秩（维数）固定，而新框架允许比较不同维数的代数。

Conclusion: 本文建立的奇点理论退化层次统一并推广了已有的代数退化概念，提供了基于自同构群和Thom多项式的算法化判定方法，为Artin代数的分类和退化结构研究开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We study the degeneration hierarchy of commutative, associative, finite-dimensional complex Artin algebras. Instead of studying degenerations in the Hilbert scheme, we introduce a singularity-theoretic notion of degeneration based on the correspondence between singularities of stable map germs and local algebras. This leads to a natural partially ordered set, the stable hierarchy, in which one algebra degenerates to another if nearby singularities realize the latter.
  Our first main result is that, in a wide range of dimensions, this hierarchy can be determined purely from symmetry data, namely from the automorphism groups of the algebras or singularities. The key tool is the theory of certain equivariant characteristic classes called Thom polynomials of multisingularities, established by Kazarian. Suitable substitutions into these polynomials completely characterize the hierarchy. As a consequence, the computation of degeneration posets becomes algorithmic in nature.
  In our second main result, we prove that our singularity-theoretic hierarchy extends the algebraic hierarchy obtained from deformation theory. While deformation theory requires the dimension (rank) to be fixed, our hierarchy generalizes this framework by comparing algebras of varying dimensions.

</details>
